Name him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**. **I will make my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]] with him**, and he will become a great nation. I will make **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/ishmael|Ishmael]]** a great nation, too, but my covenant will be with Isaac.” Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** changed **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abram's]]** name to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, which means “**father of many**.” God also changed Sarai's name to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sarah|Sarah]]**, which means “**princess**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(God continues to speak to Abram.)


    * 


**son of promise**  - Isaac would be the son that God promised to Sarai and Abram. He would also be the son that God would use to give Abram many descendants.
    * 


**I will make my covenant with him**  - This would be the same covenant that God made with Abram.
    * 


**father of many**  - As God had promised, Abraham would become the ancestor of many people who would even become many nations.
    * 


**princess**  - A princess is a daughter of a king. The names Sarai and Sarah apparently both meant “princess.” But God changed her name to signify that she would be the mother of many nations, and some of her descendants would be kings.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-05|>>]]**


===== Birth of Isaac [05-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-05-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5b2c7a?nolink&640x360}}


That day **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/circumcise|circumcised]]****all the males in his household**. About a year later, when Abraham was 100 years old and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sarah|Sarah]]** was 90, Sarah gave birth to Abraham's **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**. They named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** as **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had told them to do.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**all the males in his household**  - This means all of the men and boys that Abraham was responsible for, including his male servants, young and old.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-06|>>]]**


===== Test of Faith [05-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-05-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3debb4?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** was a young man, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] tested [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham's]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faith|faith]]** by saying, “Take Isaac, your only **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**, and **kill him**  as a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]** to me.” Again Abraham **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** God and **prepared to sacrifice**  his son.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God tested Abraham's faith**  - God wanted Abraham to show that he was completely submitted to God, that he would obey whatever God told him to do.
    * 


**kill him**  - God did not want human sacrifice. God wanted to see that Abraham loved God more than he loved his son and would obey God even when God told him to give his son back to God.
    * 


**prepared to sacrifice**  - Abraham got ready to sacrifice his son. God stopped him before he killed his son.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-07|>>]]**


===== God Will Provide [05-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-05-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5ac348?nolink&640x360}}


As **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]****walked to the place of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]**, Isaac asked, “Father, we have **wood for the sacrifice**, but where is **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb]]**?” Abraham replied, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** will provide the lamb for the sacrifice, my son.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**walked to the place of sacrifice**  - God had told Abraham to sacrifice Isaac on a special high hill that was about three days' walk from where they lived.
    * 


**wood for the sacrifice**  - For a sacrifice, normally the lamb was killed and then placed on top of wood so that the wood and the lamb could be burned up with fire.
    * 


**the lamb**  - A young sheep or goat would be the normal animal for a sacrifice.
    * 


**provide**  - Abraham may have believed that Isaac was the “lamb” that God provided, although God fulfilled Abraham's words by providing a ram to sacrifice in Isaac's place.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-08|>>]]**


===== The Sacrifice [05-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-05-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2c727f?nolink&640x360}}


When they reached the place of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** tied up his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** and laid him on an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/altar|altar]]**. He was about to **kill his son**  when **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said, “**Stop! Do not hurt the boy!**  Now I know that **you fear me**  because you did not keep **your only son**  from me.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**kill his son**  - God did not want human sacrifice. God wanted to see that Abraham loved God more than he loved his son and would obey God even when God told him to give his son back to God.
    * 


**Stop! Do no hurt the boy!**  - God protected Isaac and kept Abraham from killing him.
    * 


**you fear me**  - Abraham feared God, which included respect and reverence for God. Because of those things, he obeyed God.
    * 


**your only son**  - Ishmael was also Abraham's son, but Isaac was the only son of Abraham and Sarah. God's covenant was with Isaac and it was through Isaac that God would fulfill his promise.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-09|>>]]**


===== The Ram [05-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-05-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=014ddb?nolink&640x360}}


Nearby **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** saw **a ram**  that was stuck in a bush. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] had provided the ram**to be the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]** instead of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**. Abraham happily offered the ram as a sacrifice.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a ram**  - A ram is a male goat. Goats were one of the animals that people could sacrifice to God.
    * 


**God had provided the ram**  - Just at the right moment, God caused the ram to be stuck in the bush.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-10|>>]]**


===== The Blessing [05-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-05-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b23a8a?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, “Because you were willing to give me everything, even **your only [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**, I **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promise]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|bless]]** you. Your **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]** will be more than **the stars in the sky**. Because you have **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** me, **all the families of the world**  will be **blessed through your family**.”


//A Bible story from: Genesis 16-22//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**your only son**  - See explanation in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-08|[05-08]]]**.
    * 


**the stars in the sky**  - See explanation in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__04-05|[04-05]]]**.
    * 


**all the families of the world**  - Here, “families” refers to the larger distinct groups of people on earth, rather than to each set of parents and children.
    * 


**blessed through your family**  - Here, “family” refers to the many descendants that Abraham would have. The future generations of the world would be blessed through Abraham's descendants. The greatest blessing would come many generations later through God's chosen servant, the Messiah.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/05-the-son-of-promise|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-01|>>]]**


===== A Wife for Isaac [06-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d016db?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** was very old, his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, had grown to be a man. So Abraham **sent one of his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]] back****to the land**  where his relatives lived **to bring back a wife for his son, Isaac**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**sent one of his servants back**  – This could be translated as, “told one of his servants to go back.” The word “back” means that the servant would be going to the same place where Abraham used to live long ago before he came to Canaan. Make sure the translation of this phrase makes that clear.
    * 


**to the land**  - This land was east of where Abraham was now living.
    * 


**to bring back a wife for his son, Isaac**  - This could be translated as, “to bring back an unmarried woman for his son, Isaac, to marry”.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__05-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-02|>>]]**


===== Finding Rebekah [06-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a6cb0e?nolink&640x360}}


After a very long journey to the land where **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham's]]** relatives lived, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** led the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]]**. She was the **granddaughter of Abraham's brother**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**granddaughter of Abraham's brother**  - Specifically, she was the daughter of Abraham's brother's son. Her grandfather was Abraham's brother.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-03|>>]]**


===== Isaac Married Rebekah [06-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e3751a?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]] agreed**to leave her family and go back with the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servant]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac's]]** home. Isaac married her as soon as she arrived.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Rebekah agreed**  - Even though Rebekah's parents were arranging her marriage, they did not force her to go marry Isaac.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-04|>>]]**


===== Rebekah Was Childless [06-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6a5f26?nolink&640x360}}


After a long time, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** died and all of **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promises]] that [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] had made to him in the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]] were passed on**to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**. God had promised that Abraham would have **countless [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]**, but Isaac's wife, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]]**, could not have children.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the promises … were passed on**  - The promises of the covenant that God made with Abraham were not for him only, but also for his descendants.
    * 


**countless**  - This could also be translated as, “very many.” The word “countless” means there would be so many descendants that people would not be able to count them.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-05|>>]]**


===== Rebekah Became Pregnant [06-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=83bdfc?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** prayed for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** allowed her to get pregnant with twins. The two babies struggled with each other while they were still **in Rebekah's womb**, so Rebekah asked God what was happening.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**in Rebekah's womb**  - That is, “inside her.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-06|>>]]**


===== Two Nations [06-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=134505?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]]**, “Two nations will come **from the two sons**  inside of you. **They will struggle with each other**  and **the older [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** will **serve the younger one**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**from the two sons**  - That is, “from the descendants of the two sons.”
    * 


**They will struggle with each other**  - Both the two sons and the nations that will come from them will continually fight with each other. Compare to **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-05|[06-05]]]**.
    * 


**the older son**  - Even though the babies were twins, the baby that came out first would be treated as the older son.
    * 


**serve the younger one**  – This could be translated as, “the older son will have to do what the younger one tells him to do.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-07|>>]]**


===== Twins Were Born [06-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-06-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=db8307?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah's]] babies were born**, **the older [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** came out **red**  and **hairy**, and they named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]**. Then **the younger son**  came out holding on to Esau's heel, and they named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**.


//A Bible story from: Genesis 24:1-25:26//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Rebekah's babies were born**  - Some languages have a more indirect way of saying this such as, “when Rebekah saw and took them” or, “when Rebekah brought them to light.”
    * 


**the older son … the younger son**  - This could be translated as, “the first son to come out … the second son to come out.” Make sure that the way “older” and “younger” are translated still communicates that the boys were twins.
    * 


**red**  - This may mean that his skin was very red or that the hair on his body was red.
    * 


**hairy**  - Esau had a lot of hair on his body. You could say, “the older son's body was red, with lots of hair.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/06-god-provides-for-isaac|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-01|>>]]**


===== The Boys Grew Up [07-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cbfa35?nolink&640x360}}


As the boys grew up, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]] loved to stay at home**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]] loved to hunt**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]] loved Jacob**, **but [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]] loved Esau**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**loved to stay at home … loved to hunt**  - Some languages will use a word for “love” here that is different from the one used for, “Rebekah loved Jacob.” For example, this could be translated as, “liked to stay at home … liked to hunt” or, “preferred to stay at home … preferred to hunt.”
    * 


**at home**  - This expression refers to the area around the family dwellings. Jacob preferred to stay close to the tents where they lived. Some languages have a special expression for, “at home.”
    * 


**Rebekah loved Jacob, but Isaac loved Esau**  - This could be translated as, “Rebekah was more fond of Jacob, and Isaac was more fond of Esau.” This does not necessarily mean that Rebekah and Isaac did not love the other son, but that each parent had a favorite.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-02|>>]]**


===== Esau Sold His Rights [07-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a9d945?nolink&640x360}}


One day, when **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]** came back from hunting, he was very hungry. Esau said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**, “Please **give me some of the food**  you have made.” Jacob responded, “First, **give me your rights as the oldest son**.” So Esau gave Jacob his **rights as the oldest son**. Then Jacob gave him some food.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**give me some of the food … give me your rights**  – Some languages may prefer to use two different words for “give” here. This would also apply to, “Esau gave … Jacob gave” in the last two sentences.
    * 


**rights as the oldest son**  - According to their custom, since Esau was the oldest son, he should have been the one to receive twice as much of their father's wealth when their father died. Jacob thought of a way to take these rights of the oldest son from Esau.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-03|>>]]**


===== Rebekah and Jacob Tricked Isaac [07-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9d1775?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** wanted to **give his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessing]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]**. But before he did, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]] tricked him**by having Jacob **pretend**  to be Esau. Isaac was old and could no longer see. So Jacob put on Esau’s clothes and put **goatskins**  on his neck and hands.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**give his blessing**  - It was customary for fathers to formally express their desire for good things to happen to their children. Normally the older son received the best promise. Isaac wanted this extra prosperity to happen to Esau.
    * 


**tricked him**  - The word “trick” means to do something to deliberately deceive someone. Rebekah came up with a plan to deceive Isaac into giving Jacob the special blessing instead of Esau.
    * 


**pretend**  - The word “pretend” shows how Jacob would deceive his father (who had very poor eyesight in his old age).
    * 


**goatskins**  - The hairiness of the goatskins would make Jacob feel like Esau.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-04|>>]]**


===== Isaac Blessed Jacob [07-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2e97b5?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]] came to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** and said, “I am **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]**. I have come so that you can **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|bless]]** me.” When Isaac felt the goat hair and smelled the clothes, **he thought it was Esau**  and blessed him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Jacob came to Isaac**  - In some languages it might be more natural to say, “Jacob went to Isaac.”
    * 


**he thought it was Esau**  - He thought that the person he was touching and smelling was Esau.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-05|>>]]**


===== Esau Hated Jacob [07-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cd008d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]** hated **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** because Jacob had stolen his **rights as oldest son**  and also **his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessing]]**. So he planned to kill Jacob after their father died.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**rights as oldest son**  - Jacob found a way to get the larger portion of their father's wealth that should have gone to Esau as the older son. See also note on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-02|[07-02]]]**.
    * 


**his blessing**  - Jacob also tricked their father into giving him the promise of extra prosperity that Isaac intended to give to Esau. See also note on **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-03|[07-03]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-06|>>]]**


===== Isaac Sent Jacob Away [07-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=175ede?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah]]** heard of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau’s]] plan**. So **she and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]] sent [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]] far away to live with her relatives**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Esau's plan**  - Esau's plan was to kill Jacob after his father died.
    * 


**she and Isaac sent Jacob**  – Rebekah wanted to protect Jacob from Esau so she talked to Isaac about sending Jacob away.
    * 


**far away to live with her relatives**  - This was the same place where Rebekah was living when Abraham's servant got her to be Isaac's wife. To make this clear, you could add, “relatives in the same land where she used to live.” The land was to the east, several hundred miles away.
    * 


**her relatives**  - This could also be translated as, “their relatives.” Since Abraham's brother was Rebekah's grandfather, her relatives were also Isaac's relatives.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-07|>>]]**


===== Jacob Prospered [07-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ba9d78?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** lived with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebekah|Rebekah's]]** relatives for many years. During that time he married and had twelve sons and a daughter. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** made him very **wealthy**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wealthy**  – This included money, large herds of animals and other possessions.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-08|>>]]**


===== Jacob Returned Home [07-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3486cf?nolink&640x360}}


**After twenty years**  away from his home in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** returned there with his family, his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]**, and all his herds of animals.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**after twenty years**  - Jacob had lived for twenty years in the land where his mother was from. If that is not clear you could say, “After twenty years living in the land where his relatives were.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-09|>>]]**


===== Jacob Met Esau [07-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=61885d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** was very afraid because he thought **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]** still wanted to kill him. So he sent many herds of animals to Esau as a gift. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|servants]]** who brought the animals said to Esau, “**Your servant, Jacob**, is giving you these animals. He is coming soon.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**your servant, Jacob**  - Jacob was not actually Esau's servant. But Jacob told his servants to say this because he wanted to show Esau that he was coming to him humbly and respectfully, so that Esau would no longer be angry with him.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-10|>>]]**


===== The Brothers Were Reunited [07-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-07-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a32413?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/esau|Esau]]** had already **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgiven]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**, and they were happy to see each other again. Jacob then **lived [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peacefully]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**. Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]** died, and Jacob and Esau **buried him**. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promises]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had promised to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** now **passed on from Isaac to Jacob**.


//A Bible story from: Genesis 25:27-33:20//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**lived peacefully**  - This refers to the fact that Esau and Jacob were not angry at each other and did not fight with each other.
    * 


**buried him**  - This could mean that they dug a hole in the ground, placed Isaac's body in it, and covered the hole with dirt or stones. Or it could mean that they placed Isaac's body in a cave and covered the opening.
    * 


**covenant promises**  - These were the promises that God made in his covenant with Abraham.
    * 


**passed on from Isaac to Jacob**  - The promises went from Abraham to his son Isaac, and now to Isaac's son Jacob. Esau did not receive the promises. See also **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-04|[06-04]]]**.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/07-god-blesses-jacob|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-01|>>]]**


===== Joseph, the Favorite Son [08-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=9a7466?nolink&640x360}}


Many years later, when **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** was an old man, he **sent**  his **favorite son**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]**, to **check on**  his **brothers**  who were **taking care of the herds**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**sent**  – This word means that Jacob told Joseph to go and Joseph went.
    * 


**favorite son**  - This could be translated as, “the son he loved more than any of his other children.”
    * 


**check on**  - This means that Joseph is to go and see if everything is all right with his brothers. Some languages might say something like, “to see his brothers' well-being.”
    * 


**brothers**  - These were Joseph's older brothers.
    * 


**taking care of the herds**  – Since this was several days' journey away, it may be necessary to say, “who were far away taking care of.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-02|>>]]**


===== Joseph Was Sold as a Slave [08-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7d2caa?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph’s]]** brothers hated him because their father loved him most and because Joseph had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/dream|dreamed]]** that he would be their ruler. When Joseph **came to his brothers**, they **kidnapped**  him and sold him to some **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave]] traders**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**came to his brothers**  – Another way this could be translated is, “reached the place where his brothers were.”
    * 


**kidnapped**  - They took him against his will. It was not right for them to do this.
    * 


**slave traders**  - These were people who made a business of buying people from one owner and selling them as slaves to another owner.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-03|>>]]**


===== The Brothers' Lie [08-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7a3e6c?nolink&640x360}}


Before **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph’s]]** brothers returned home, they tore Joseph’s robe and dipped it in **goat's blood**. Then they showed the robe to their father so he would think that a wild animal had killed Joseph. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** was very sad.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**goat's blood**  - The brothers wanted Jacob to think that the blood on the clothes was Joseph's blood.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-04|>>]]**


===== Joseph in Egypt [08-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4b1a6c?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave]]** traders took **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. Egypt was a large, powerful country located along the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nile-river|Nile River]]**. The slave traders sold Joseph as a slave to a wealthy **government official**. Joseph served his master well, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]]** Joseph.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**government official**  - This was a person who was part of the Egyptian government. Another way to say this would be, “a leader in Egypt's government.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-05|>>]]**


===== Joseph in Prison [08-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f59b85?nolink&640x360}}


His master’s wife **tried to sleep with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]**, but Joseph refused to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]] against [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** in this way. She became angry and falsely accused Joseph so that he was arrested and sent to prison. Even in prison, Joseph **remained [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]] to God**, and God **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]]** him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**tried to sleep with Joseph**  – Another way to say this would be, “tried to seduce Joseph to have sex with her.” To “sleep with” is a way of expressing this in order not to be crude or offensive.
    * 


**sin against God**  - It is against God's law for people to have sex if they are not married to each other. Joseph did not want to sin by disobeying God's law.
    * 


**remained faithful to God**  - Another way to say this would be, “continued to obey God.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-06|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh's Dream [08-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=96601c?nolink&640x360}}


After two years, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** was still in prison, even though he was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/innocent|innocent]]**. One night, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]**, which is what the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** called their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|kings]]**, had two **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/dream|dreams]]** that **disturbed him greatly**. None of **his advisors**  could tell him the **meaning of the dreams**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**disturbed him greatly**  – This means that the king felt very afraid and confused (because of what he had seen in the dreams).
    * 


**his advisors**  - These were men with special powers and knowledge who could sometimes tell what dreams meant. Some translations refer to them as, “wise men.”
    * 


**meaning of the dreams**  - People in Egypt believed that dreams were messages from the gods telling them about what would happen in the future. God used Pharaoh's dreams to tell him what would happen.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-07|>>]]**


===== Joseph Interpreted the Dream [08-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6866a3?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had given **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** the ability to **interpret [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/dream|dreams]]**, so **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]] had Joseph brought to him**from the prison. Joseph interpreted the dreams for him and said, “**God is going to send**  seven years of plentiful harvests, followed by seven years of **famine**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**interpret dreams**  - To “interpret” is to tell what something means. So Joseph was able to tell people what their dreams meant.
    * 


**had Joseph brought to him**  - Another way to say this would be, “ordered his servants to bring Joseph to him.”
    * 


**God is going to send**  - God will cause the crops to grow well for seven years, and after that He will cause them to produce very little food so that the people and animals will not have enough to eat.
    * 


**famine**  - The gardens and fields would produce so little food that people and animals would not have enough to eat.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-08|>>]]**


===== Joseph Ruled Egypt [08-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=64f8a8?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** was so **impressed with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** that he appointed him to be the **second most powerful man**  in all of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**!


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**impressed with**  - Pharaoh was amazed by Joseph's wisdom and felt respect for him; he trusted Joseph to make wise decisions that would benefit the people. It may be clearer to say, “impressed with Joseph's wisdom.”
    * 


**second most powerful man**  - Pharaoh made Joseph a very powerful and important ruler over all of Egypt. Only Pharaoh was more powerful and important than Joseph.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-09|>>]]**


===== Joseph Stored Up Food [08-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cdb66c?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** told the people to **store up large amounts of food**  during the seven years of good harvests. Then Joseph sold the food to the people when the seven years of **famine**  came so they would have enough to eat.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**store up large amounts of food**  - They took food from the abundant harvests to the cities and stored it there. The food then belonged to Pharaoh.
    * 


**famine**  - See how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-07|[08-07]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-10|>>]]**


===== The Famine [08-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ab80d9?nolink&640x360}}


**The famine was severe**  not only in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**, but also in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]** where **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** and his family lived.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Egypt, but also Canaan**  – For some languages it may be clearer or more natural to say, “the country of Egypt, but also the land of Canaan.”
    * 


**The famine was severe**  - The famine was very bad. There was very little food and many people outside of Egypt were starving.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-11|>>]]**


===== The Brothers Bought Food [08-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=236cd3?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** sent **his older sons**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** to buy food. The brothers **did not recognize [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** when they stood before him to buy food. But Joseph recognized them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**his older sons**  - These were Joseph's older brothers who had sold him into slavery.
    * 


**did not recognize Joseph**  - They did not know that the man was Joseph, because now Joseph was much older than when they last saw him, and he was dressed as an Egyptian ruler.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-12|>>]]**


===== Joseph Met His Brothers [08-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ffa3c0?nolink&640x360}}


After **testing his brothers**  to see **if they had changed**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** said to them, “I am your brother, Joseph! **Do not be afraid**. You tried to do **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|evil]]** when you sold me as a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave]]**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** used the **evil for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/good|good]]**! Come and live in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** so I can provide for you and your families.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**testing his brothers**  - Joseph placed his older brothers in a difficult situation to see if they would protect their youngest brother, or treat him as badly as they had treated Joseph. When they protected their youngest brother, Joseph knew they had changed.
    * 


**if they had changed**  - Another way to say this would be, “if they were different than they used to be.” Years ago Joseph's brothers sold him into slavery. Joseph wanted to find out if they would now do what was right.
    * 


**do not be afraid**  - Another way to say this would be, “You do not need to fear any punishment from me.” Joseph's brothers were afraid because they had greatly wronged Joseph and now as a great ruler he had the power to punish them. Joseph could refuse to sell them food, or even put them in prison or kill them.
    * 


**evil for good**  - Joseph's brothers did an evil thing when they sold Joseph as a slave and he was taken to Egypt. But God allowed this so that Joseph could save thousands of people from starving during the famine, including his own family. This was a very good thing.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-13|>>]]**


===== Joseph Was Alive [08-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=140f5a?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph's]]** brothers returned home and told their father, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**, that Joseph was still alive, he was very happy.


==== Translation Notes: ====


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 


**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-14|>>]]**


===== Jacob Went to Egypt [08-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3d2029?nolink&640x360}}


**Even though [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]] was an old man, he moved to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** with all of his family, and they all lived there. **Before Jacob died**, he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]]** each of his sons.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Even though Jacob was an old man, he moved to Egypt**  - Egypt was a great distance away from Canaan, and it would have been difficult for an elderly man to walk or ride a cart that far.
    * 


**Before Jacob died**  - Jacob died in Egypt. He did not get to return to Canaan, the land God had promised to give to him and his descendants.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-15|>>]]**


===== The Twelve Sons [08-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-08-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c912c8?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promises]]** that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** gave to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]** were **passed on to**  **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, then to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**, and then to Jacob’s twelve sons and their families. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]** of the twelve sons became the **twelve tribes of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**.


//A Bible story from: Genesis 37-50//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**covenant promises**  - Long ago God made an agreement with Abraham and promised him that he would give him many descendants; they would possess the land of Canaan and become a great nation. God also promised that all peoples would be blessed through Abraham's line. See also **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__07-10|[07-10]]]**.
    * 


**passed on to**  - Another way to say this would be, “passed down to” or, “given to” or, “applied to.” God's promise to Abraham was also for Abraham's children, grandchildren and all the rest of his descendants. See also **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__06-04|[06-04]]]**.
    * 


**twelve tribes of Israel**  - God had promised Abraham, Isaac and Jacob that their descendants would become a great nation. God later changed Jacob's name to Israel. The descendants of Jacob's 12 sons became 12 great tribes. These 12 tribes made up the ancient nation called Israel, which was named by Jacob's new name.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/08-god-saves-joseph-and-his-family|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-01|>>]]**


===== The Israelites [09-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8d1a77?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** died, all of his relatives stayed in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. They and their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]** continued to live there for many years and had many children. They were called the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**called the Israelites**  - The people group that descended from Jacob was called “Israel,” which is the name that God gave to Jacob. The people from that group were called “Israelites.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__08-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-02|>>]]**


===== A New Pharaoh [09-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=776a2c?nolink&640x360}}


After hundreds of years, the number of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** had become very large. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** no longer remembered **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joseph|Joseph]]** and all he had done to help them. They became afraid of the Israelites because there were so many of them. So the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** who was ruling Egypt at that time **made the Israelites [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]]** to the Egyptians.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Pharaoh**  – “Pharaoh” is an Egyptian word that refers to their king. This Pharaoh was probably the son of a former Pharaoh who had died, who may have been a descendant of the Pharaoh that Joseph knew.
    * 


**made the Israelites slaves**  - That is, “forced the Israelites to do hard labor against their will and treated them very harshly.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-03|>>]]**


===== Hard Labor [09-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=601cbc?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** forced the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** to build many buildings and even whole cities. The hard work made their lives **miserable**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]] them**, and they had even more children.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**miserable**  – This means that they suffered terribly because of how harshly they were treated and how hard they were forced to work. They also felt very discouraged.
    * 


**God blessed them**  - God took care of them, helping them endure the severe treatment and even caused them to become more numerous by giving them children.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-04|>>]]**


===== Kill the Baby Boys [09-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=41878e?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]] saw**that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** were having many babies, so he ordered his people to kill all Israelite baby boys by throwing them into the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nile-river|Nile River]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**saw**  – Another way to say this would be, “realized” or, “knew.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-05|>>]]**


===== The Birth of Moses [09-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=85aef2?nolink&640x360}}


A certain **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]]** woman gave birth to a baby boy. She and her husband hid the baby for **as long as they could**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**as long as they could**  - They hid the baby from the Egyptians until it became too difficult to keep him safely hidden in their home.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-06|>>]]**


===== Moses in a Basket [09-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=456c96?nolink&640x360}}


When the boy's parents could no longer hide him, they put him in a **floating basket among the reeds along the edge of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nile-river|Nile River]]** in order to save him from being killed. His older sister watched to see what would happen to him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-07|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh's Daughter [09-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=03d4f0?nolink&640x360}}


A daughter of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** saw the basket and looked inside. When she saw the baby, she **took him as her own [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]**. She hired an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]]** woman **to nurse him**  without realizing the woman was the baby’s own mother. When the child was old enough that he no longer needed his mother's milk, she returned him to Pharaoh’s daughter, who named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**took him as her own son**  - She was a princess. When she made him her son, he became a prince of Egypt.
    * 


**to nurse him**  - Another way to say this would be, “to breastfeed him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-08|>>]]**


===== An Egyptian Beat a Slave [09-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=89e769?nolink&640x360}}


One day, when **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** had **grown up**, he saw an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]]** beating an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slave]]**. Moses tried to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** his **fellow Israelite**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**grown up**  - Another way to say this would be, “grown into a man.”
    * 


**fellow Israelite**  - This phrase refers to the Israelite slave. The word “fellow” here indicates that Moses was also an Israelite. Although the daughter of the Egyptian Pharaoh raised Moses, Moses remembered that he was really an Israelite.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-09|>>]]**


===== Moses Killed an Egyptian [09-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6197a8?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** thought nobody would see, he killed the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]]** and buried his body. But someone saw what Moses had done.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-10|>>]]**


===== Moses Fled from Egypt [09-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e76642?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** heard what **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** had done, he tried to kill him. Moses ran away from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** to the **wilderness**  where he would be safe from Pharaoh's soldiers.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wilderness**  - The wilderness was a large area that was rocky and dry. The land there was not good for growing food and few people lived there.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-11|>>]]**


===== Moses in the Wilderness [09-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5483dc?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** became a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/shepherd|shepherd]]** in the **wilderness**  far away from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. He married a woman from that place and had two sons.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**wilderness**  - See how you translated this in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-10|[09-10]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-12|>>]]**


===== The Burning Bush [09-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a81d19?nolink&640x360}}


One day while **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** was **taking care of his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sheep|sheep]]**, he saw a bush that was on fire. But the **bush did not burn up**. Moses went towards the bush to be able to see it better. As he approached the burning bush, **the voice of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] said**, “Moses, **take off your shoes**. You are standing on **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy|holy]] ground**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**taking care of his sheep**  - This means he was doing the work of a shepherd to guide the sheep to grass and water, and to protect them. It could be translated as, “tending the sheep.”
    * 


**bush did not burn up**  - God made the bush full of fire, but the fire did not damage the bush.
    * 


**the voice of God said**  - This could be translated as, “God said out loud.” Moses heard God speak, but he did not see God.
    * 


**take off your shoes**  - God wanted him to take off his shoes to show that he greatly respected God. To make clear the reason for this, you could say, “take off your shoes, because you are on holy ground.”
    * 


**holy ground**  - It was holy in the sense that God set it apart from the ordinary land and made it to be a special place where He would reveal Himself.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-13|>>]]**


===== God Sent Moses to Egypt [09-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0ed684?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said, “I have seen the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/suffer|suffering]] of my people**. I will send you to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** so that you can **bring the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]] out of their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slavery]] in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. I will give them the land of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**, the land I **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**suffering of my people**  - This could be translated as, “the very harsh treatment that my people are experiencing. Some languages might translate this as, “how the Egyptians are giving my people terrible pain.”
    * 


**my people**  - This refers to the Israelites. God had made a covenant with Abraham and his descendants that He would bless them and make them into a great nation. Through this covenant, the Israelites became God's own people.
    * 


**bring … out of their slavery in Egypt**  - This can be translated as, “set them free from being slaves in Egypt” or, “bring them out of Egypt where they are now slaves.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-14|>>]]**


===== The Name of God [09-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bd357f?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** asked, “What if **the people**  want to know who sent me, what should I say?” **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said, “**I AM WHO I AM**. Tell them, ‘**I AM**  has sent me to you.’ Also tell them, 'I am **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/yahweh|Yahweh]]**, the God of your ancestors **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**.' This is **my name**  forever.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the people**  - See “my people” in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-13|[09-13]]]**.
    * 


**I AM WHO I AM**  - This description shows that God can only be defined by himself, not by anything else that we know of, and he cannot be compared to anyone else.
    * 


**I AM**  - This name emphasizes that God is the only one who has always lived and always will live.
    * 


**my name**  - The name that God told Moses and all of Israel to use for him is “Yahweh,” which is related to “I AM” and appears to mean, “HE IS.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-15|>>]]**


===== Aaron Helped Moses [09-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-09-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=17b434?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]] was afraid and did not want to go**to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** because he thought he could not speak well, so **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** sent **Moses’ brother, [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]**, to help him. God warned Moses and Aaron that Pharaoh would be **stubborn**.


//A Bible story from: Exodus 1-4//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**was afraid and did not want to go**  - Moses knew that Pharaoh wanted to kill him, and he did not believe that he could do what God wanted him to do.
    * 


**Moses' brother, Aaron**  - Aaron was Moses's actual brother from his Israelite mother and father. Aaron would have been at least several years older than Moses.
    * 


**stubborn**  - This means the Pharaoh would refuse to obey God. You may also want to add, “stubborn and refuse to listen (or obey).”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/09-god-calls-moses|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-01|>>]]**


===== Let My People Go! [10-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4e8aaf?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]** went **to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]**. They said, “This is what the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** says, ‘**Let my people go**!’” Pharaoh did not **listen to**  them. Instead of letting the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** go free, he forced them to work even harder!


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**to Pharaoh**  – It may be clearer to say, “to Pharaoh's palace to talk to him.”
    * 


**God of Israel**  - This could be translated as, “God, who chose the Israelites to be his people” or, “God, who rules the people of Israel” or, “the God whom the Israelites worship.”
    * 


**Let My people go**  – Another way to say this would be, “Allow My people to go free” or, “Free My people to leave Egypt.”
    * 


**my people**  - See “my people” in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-13|[09-13]]]**.
    * 


**listen to**  – This could be translated as “heed” or, “obey.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-02|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh Refused to Obey [10-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=735543?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** kept refusing to let **the people**  go, so **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** sent **ten terrible plagues**  on **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. Through these plagues, God showed Pharaoh that he is more powerful than Pharaoh and **all of Egypt's [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|gods]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the people**  - This refers to the people of Israel, also called, “the Israelites.”
    * 


**ten terrible plagues**  - A plague is something very bad or terrible that happens to someone or something. A plague usually refers to something that affects many people or happens over a large geographic area. Another word for “plague” would be “disaster.”
    * 


**all of Egypt's gods**  - It may be more clear to say, “all the gods that the Egyptian people worshiped.” The people of Egypt worshiped many different false gods. These false gods were either spirit beings that the God of Israel created, or they did not actually exist.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-03|>>]]**


===== The Water Became Blood [10-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e4a37a?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] turned the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nile-river|Nile River]] into blood**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** still would not let the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** go.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**turned the Nile River into blood**  - Some languages may need to say, “turned the water in the Nile River into blood.” Instead of water in the river there was blood, so the fish died and the people had no water to drink.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-04|>>]]**


===== The Frogs [10-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=064694?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] sent frogs all over [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/beg|begged]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** to take away the frogs. But after all the frogs died, Pharaoh **hardened his heart**  and would not let the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** leave Egypt.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God sent frogs all over Egypt**  - This could be translated as, “God caused many frogs to appear throughout Egypt.”
    * 


**hardened his heart**  - He became stubborn again and refused to obey God.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-05|>>]]**


===== The Gnats and the Flies [10-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=80b494?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] sent a plague**of **gnats**. Then he sent a plague of **flies**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** called **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]** and told them that if they stopped the plague, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** could leave Egypt. When Moses prayed, God removed all the flies from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. But Pharaoh **hardened his heart**  and would not let the people go free.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God sent a plague**  – This could be translated as, “God caused there to be a plague” or, “God caused a plague (of gnats) to come over the land of Egypt.”
    * 


**gnats**  - These were tiny, biting insects flying in large swarms, annoying and landing on all the people and animals of Egypt.
    * 


**flies**  - These were much bigger flying insects that were both annoying and destructive. There were so many of these flies that they covered everything, even filling the Egyptians' houses.
    * 


**hardened his heart**  - See note in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-04|[10-04]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-06|>>]]**


===== The Animals Died [10-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=421728?nolink&640x360}}


Next, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** caused all the farm animals that belonged to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** to get sick and die. But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh’s]] heart was hardened**, and he would not let the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** go.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**farm animals**  - This refers to large animals that the Egyptians used to help them in their work, such as horses, donkeys, camels, cattle, sheep, and goats.
    *
