**heart was hardened**  - See note in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-04|[10-04]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-07|>>]]**


===== The Painful Sores [10-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5b6af8?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** to throw ashes into the air in front of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]**. When he did, painful skin sores appeared on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]**, but not on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]**. **God hardened Pharaoh's heart**, and Pharaoh would not let the Israelites go free.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God hardened Pharaoh's heart**  - God caused Pharaoh to continue to be stubborn. See also note in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-04|[10-04]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-08|>>]]**


===== The Hail [10-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=fab8e3?nolink&640x360}}


**After that**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] sent hail**that destroyed most of the crops in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** and killed anybody who went outside. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** called **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]** and told them, “I have **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]**. **You may go**.” So Moses **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]**, and the hail stopped falling from the sky.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**After that**  - This means, after God caused the painful sores to appear on the Egyptians' skin.
    * 


**God sent hail**  - God caused hail to fall from the sky.
    * 


**hail**  - Hail is like chunks of ice that fall down from the clouds as rain does. These chunks can be very small or very large. The larger ones will hurt or kill whatever they fall on.
    * 


**You may go**  - The word “you” refers to Moses, Aaron, and the Israelites.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-09|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh's Hard Heart [10-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e432f1?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]** again and **hardened his heart**. He would not let the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** go free.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**hardened his heart**  - See note in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-04|[10-04]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-10|>>]]**


===== The Locusts [10-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=294d4a?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** caused **swarms of locusts**  to come over **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. These **locusts**  ate all the crops that the **hail**  had not destroyed.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**swarms of locusts**  - Locusts are grasshoppers that fly together in swarms, or large groups, and that can destroy large areas of all kinds of plants and food crops by eating them.
    * 


**hail**  - Hail is like chunks of ice that fall down from the clouds as rain does.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-11|>>]]**


===== The Darkness [10-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e9c74a?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] sent darkness that lasted for three days**. It was so dark that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** could not leave their houses. But there was light where the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** lived.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God sent darkness**  - God caused darkness to cover or spread over most of Egypt. In other words, God took away the light from this part of Egypt.
    * 


**darkness that lasted for three days**  - This darkness was darker than ordinary nighttime darkness, and it continued to be totally dark for three whole days.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-12|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh Refused to Listen [10-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-10-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d21cdc?nolink&640x360}}


Even after **these nine plagues**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** still refused to let the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** go free. **Since Pharaoh would not listen**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** planned to send one last plague. **This would change Pharaoh’s mind**.


//A Bible story from: Exodus 5-10//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**these nine plagues**  - This means, “these nine disasters that God had caused.”
    * 


**Since Pharaoh would not listen**  - This could be translated as, “Since Pharaoh would not do what God was telling him to do” or, “Since Pharaoh refused to obey God.”
    * 


**This would change Pharaoh's mind**  - Another way to say this would be, “This last plague would cause Pharaoh to change how he thought about God and as a result he would let the Israelites go free.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/10-the-ten-plagues|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-01|>>]]**


===== Firstborn Males Would Die [11-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=28ca1d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** warned **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** that if he did not let the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** go, then he would kill all the **firstborn males of both people and animals**. When Pharaoh heard this he still refused to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** God.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the firstborn males of both people and animals**  - This could be translated as, “the eldest son in every family and the first male offspring of any of their animals.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__10-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-02|>>]]**


===== The Sacrifice [11-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=262bc4?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] provided**a way to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** the firstborn **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** of anyone who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** in him. Each family had to choose a **perfect [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb]]** and kill it.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God provided**  – God is the only one who could provide the way to save the Israelites' sons from death.
    * 


**perfect lamb**  - That is, “a young sheep or goat that had no blemishes or defects.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-03|>>]]**


===== Blood on the Door [11-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=80c7e2?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** to put some of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb's]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]]** around the door of their house, and to roast the meat and eat it quickly, along with bread that was **made without yeast**. He also told them to be ready to leave **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]****when they ate**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**made without yeast**  – Yeast is something that is mixed into bread dough to make bread rise as it cooks. This could be translated as, “made without something that would make it rise.” Making the bread with yeast would have taken much longer, so cooking the bread without yeast was a way to be prepared to leave Egypt quickly.
    * 


**when they ate**  – This means they needed to be prepared to leave before they started to eat.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-04|>>]]**


===== The Passover Meal [11-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=3c2391?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** did everything just as **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had commanded them to do. In the middle of the night, God went throughout **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** killing **every firstborn son**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**every firstborn son**  - This means every firstborn son of families who had not made the blood sacrifice, that is, the Egyptians. To make this clear you may want to add, “Every Egyptian firstborn son” (since all the Israelite families had put the blood on their doorposts).
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-05|>>]]**


===== Saved by the Blood [11-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c71695?nolink&640x360}}


All the houses of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]]** around the doors, so **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]****passed over**  those houses. Everybody inside them was safe. **They were [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]] because of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb's]] blood**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**passed over**  - This means that God passed by those houses and did not stop to kill anyone there. This phrase became the name of the Jewish festival, “Passover.”
    * 


**They were saved**  - God did not kill their firstborn son.
    * 


**because of the lamb's blood**  - This could be translated as, “because the lamb's blood was on their door.” God saw that they had killed their lamb as he had commanded, so he did not kill their son.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-06|>>]]**


===== Death of the Firstborn [11-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2dbde0?nolink&640x360}}


But the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]****did not [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believe]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] or obey his commands**. So God **did not pass over**  their houses. God killed every one of the Egyptians' firstborn sons.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**did not believe God or obey his commands**  – In some languages it may be more natural or clear to say, “did not believe God and so they did not obey his commands.”
    * 


**did not pass over**  - He did not pass by their houses. Rather he stopped at each house and killed their eldest son.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-07|>>]]**


===== Sorrow in Egypt [11-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2788ee?nolink&640x360}}


Every **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]]** firstborn male died, **from the firstborn of the prisoner in jail, to the firstborn of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]**. Many people in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** were crying and wailing because of their deep sadness.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**from the firstborn of the prisoner in jail, to the firstborn of Pharaoh**  - This is a way of saying that everyone's firstborn son died–from the son of the least important person to the son of the most important person, and everyone in between.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-08|>>]]**


===== Go Away! [11-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-11-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6db4f5?nolink&640x360}}


That same night, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]] called for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]] and said**, “Take the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** and leave **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]** immediately!” The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]]** people also urged the Israelites to leave immediately.


//A Bible story from: Exodus 11:1-12:32//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**called for**  – This means that Pharaoh told his servants to tell Moses and Aaron to come to him.
    * 


**and said**  – Pharaoh said the following words to Moses and Aaron after they came to him. In some languages this would be translated as, “and said to them,” or, “After they came, Pharaoh said to them.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/11-the-passover|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-01|>>]]**


===== Israel Left Egypt [12-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b7651f?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** were very happy to leave **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. **They were no longer [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]]**, and they were **going**  to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**! The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** gave the Israelites whatever they asked for, even gold and silver and other valuable things. Some people from other nations **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and went along with the Israelites as they left Egypt.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**They were no longer slaves**  - This could be translated as, “They were not slaves anymore.”
    * 


**going**  – Some languages may use a more specific word like “traveling” since they would be going a long distance to the Promised Land.
    * 


**Promised Land**  - This is the land that God had promised that he would give to Abraham's descendants.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__11-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-02|>>]]**


===== God Went before Israel [12-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=231e87?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** led them with a **tall pillar of cloud**  that went ahead of them during the day, and which became a **tall pillar of fire**  at night. God was always with them and **guided them**  as they traveled. All they had to do was follow him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**tall pillar of cloud**  - This could be translated as, “a tall cloud” or, “a cloud shaped like a pillar.”
    * 


**tall pillar of fire**  - This was a column of fire that hung or floated in the air in front of the Israelites.
    * 


**guided them**  - God showed them the way by making the pillar move along in front of them so they could follow it.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-03|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh Changed His Mind [12-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e9709a?nolink&640x360}}


**After a short time**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** and his people **changed their minds**  and wanted the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** to be their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]]** again. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** caused Pharaoh to be stubborn so that people would see he is the One True God, and understand that he, Yahweh, is more powerful than Pharaoh and his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|gods]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**After a short time**  – Probably at least two days had gone by. For that to be clear, it may be translated as, “After a few days” or, “A few days after the Israelites left Egypt.”
    * 


**changed their minds**  - This phrase means, “began to think differently than they had before.” Some languages may not have this same expression, and will express the meaning in a direct way.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-04|>>]]**


===== Pharaoh Chased Israel [12-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5911d6?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pharaoh|Pharaoh]]** and his army chased after the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** to **make them their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]] again**. When the Israelites saw the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]]** army coming, they realized **they were trapped between Pharaoh's army and the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/red-sea|Red Sea]]**. They were very afraid and cried out, “**Why did we leave [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**? We are going to die!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**they were trapped between…Red Sea**  - Another way to say this would be, “there was nowhere they could go to escape since the Egyptians were behind them and the Red Sea was in front of them.”
    * 


**Why did we leave Egypt?**  – This means, “We should not have left Egypt!” They were not really asking for reasons. Because they were afraid, in this moment they were wishing they had not left Egypt (even though it had been very difficult for them there).
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-05|>>]]**


===== God Will Fight for You [12-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cae74d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]**, “**Stop being afraid**! **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] will fight for you today and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]] you**.” Then God told Moses, “Tell the people to **move**  toward the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/red-sea|Red Sea]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God will fight for you today and save you**  - Another way to say this would be, “Today God will defeat the Egyptians for you and keep them from harming you.”
    * 


**move**  – Some languages will be more specific and say, “walk.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-06|>>]]**


===== Darkness over the Egyptians [12-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f6573c?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** moved the **pillar of cloud**  and placed it between the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** so the Egyptians **could not see**  the Israelites.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**pillar of cloud**  – See how you translated this phrase in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-02|[12-02]]]**
    * 


**could not see**  - The cloud pillar was so large and thick that the Egyptians could no longer see any of the Israelites.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-07|>>]]**


===== Moses Divided the Sea [12-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e8f558?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** to **raise his hand over the sea**  and divide the waters. Then God caused wind to push the water in the sea to the left and the right, so that a path formed through the sea.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**raise his hand over the sea**  - This could be translated as, “held out his hand over the sea”. This was a gesture to show that God was doing this miracle through Moses.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-08|>>]]**


===== Israel Crossed the Sea [12-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f9ba5d?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]****marched**  through the sea on dry ground **with a wall of water on either side of them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**marched**  - This can be translated as, “walked” or, “went.”
    * 


**with a wall of water on either side of them**  - This could be translated as, “and the water on both sides of them stood up tall and straight like a wall.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-09|>>]]**


===== Egypt Pursued Israel [12-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e07c5f?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** moved the cloud up and out of the way so that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** could see the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** escaping. The Egyptians decided to chase after them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-10|>>]]**


===== God Fought for Israel [12-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e682ac?nolink&640x360}}


So they followed the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** onto the **path through the sea**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** caused the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]****to panic**  and caused their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/chariot|chariots]]** to **get stuck**. They shouted, “Run away! God is fighting for the Israelites!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**path through the sea**  - This was the dry strip of land across the bottom of the sea, with a wall of water on each side.
    * 


**to panic**  – This could be translated as, “to get fearful and confused.”
    * 


**get stuck**  - The chariots could no longer move.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-11|>>]]**


===== The Egyptians Drowned [12-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d1f484?nolink&640x360}}


After the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** all **made it safely to the other side**  of the sea, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** to **stretch out his arm again**. When he obeyed, the **water fell on the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]] army**and **returned to its normal place**. **The whole Egyptian army**  drowned.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**made it safely to the other side**  – This could be translated as, “walked safely to the other side” or, “arrived safely on the other side” or, “walked to the other side and were safe from the Egyptians and the sea.”
    * 


**stretch out his arm again**  - This could be translated as, “lift his arm over the sea again” or, as a direct command, as in, “God told Moses, 'Stretch out your arm again.'”
    * 


**returned to its normal place**  - This could be translated as, “covered the place again where the path had been,” or “filled the whole sea again” or, “went back to where it was before God separated it.”
    * 


**The whole Egyptian army**  - This could be translated as, “everyone in Egypt's army.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-12|>>]]**


===== Israel Believed God [12-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e53ead?nolink&640x360}}


When the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** saw that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** were dead, they **trusted in [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** was **a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]] of God**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**trusted in God**  - In other words, the people now trusted that God was powerful and could protect them.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-13|>>]]**


===== Israel Rejoiced [12-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=92502c?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** also **rejoiced with much excitement**  because **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]** them **from death and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slavery]]**! Now they were **free to serve**  God. The Israelites sang many songs to celebrate their new freedom and to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praise]] God**because he saved them from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptian]]** army.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**rejoiced with much excitement**  - This could be translated as, “were very happy and they showed it enthusiastically” or, “showed it with their whole hearts” or, “with all their strength.”
    * 


**from death and slavery**  - This could be translated as, “from being killed or made slaves by the Egyptians.”
    * 


**free to serve**  - God freed, or rescued, the Israelites from being slaves in Egypt so that they could serve him.
    * 


**praise God**  - In some languages this could be translated as, “lift up God's name” or, “say that God is great.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-14|>>]]**


===== An Annual Feast [12-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-12-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=929ba6?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** commanded the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** to celebrate **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/passover|Passover]]** every year in order to **remember how God gave them victory over**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egyptians]]** and rescued them from being **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]]**. They celebrated by killing a **perfect [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/lamb|lamb]]**, eating it with **unleavened bread**.


//A Bible story from: Exodus 12:33-15:21//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the Passover**  - This could be translated as, “the Passover activities” or, “the Passover celebration” or, “the Passover meal.”
    * 


**remember how God gave them victory over**  – This could be translated as, “regularly remind themselves of how God defeated.” The word “remember” here doesn't just mean to not forget; it also means to formally commemorate something.
    * 


**perfect lamb**  - The word “perfect” here refers to a lamb with no disease or anything else wrong with it. Another way to say this might be, “a completely healthy and well-formed lamb.”
    * 


**unleavened bread**  - This is another way to say, “bread that was made without yeast.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/12-the-exodus|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-01|>>]]**


===== The Mountain at Sinai [13-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=390169?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** led the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** through the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/red-sea|Red Sea]]**, he led them through the wilderness to a mountain called **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sinai|Sinai]]**. This was the same mountain where **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** had seen the **burning bush**. The people **set up their tents**  at the **base of the mountain**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**burning bush**  - Before Moses returned to Egypt, God had spoken to him from a shrub that was on fire, but that was not burned up by the fire. See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__09-12|[09-12]]]**.
    * 


**set up their tents**  - The Israelites had to travel a great distance from Egypt to the Promised Land. So they took tents with them so that they could set them up as shelters and sleep in them along the way. Some languages could translate this as, “hung their tents.”
    * 


**base of the mountain**  – This could be translated as, “bottom of the mountain.” This refers to the area of land that is located next to the place where the ground starts to slant upward to form a mountain.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-02|>>]]**


===== God Called Israel [13-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c8d4e3?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and the people of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**, “If you will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** me and **keep my [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]]**, **you will be my prized possession**, a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdom]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priests]]**, and a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy|holy]] nation**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**keep my covenant**  - This could be translated as, “do what my covenant requires you to do.” Obeying and keeping the covenant are not two different things. One way to make this clear would be to say, “obey me by keeping my covenant.” God will soon tell them what his covenant requires.
    * 


**my prized possession**  - This could be translated as, “You will be my possession that I value most” or, “You will be the people that I treasure more than any other group of people” or, “You will be my own precious people.”
    * 


**You will be…a kingdom of priests**  - This could be translated as, “I will be your king and you will be like priests.” The Israelites were supposed to teach the other nations about God and be a mediator between God and the nations just as there were priests in the nation of Israel to go between God and the Israelites.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-03|>>]]**


===== Moses Met God [13-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ce527b?nolink&640x360}}


**Three days later**, after the people had **prepared themselves spiritually**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** came down on top of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sinai|Mount Sinai]]** with thunder, lightning, smoke, and a **loud trumpet blast**. **Only [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]] was allowed to go up**the mountain.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Three days later**  - In other words, three days after they arrived at Mount Sinai and God first spoke to them.
    * 


**prepared themselves spiritually**  - This refers to ceremonial cleansing in preparation to meet with God. This could be translated as, “got ready to meet with God” or, “prepared themselves to meet with God.”
    * 


**loud trumpet blast**  - This could be translated as, “and a loud sound came from a horn” or, “and a horn was blown and it made a loud sound” or, “and they heard the loud sound of a horn blowing.” Trumpets were made out of ram's horns. They were used that day to call the people to gather at the mountain and meet with God.
    * 


**Only Moses was allowed to go up**  - This could be translated as, “God permitted Moses to go up, but he did not permit anyone else to go up.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-04|>>]]**


===== I Am Your God [13-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=800c9b?nolink&640x360}}


**Then [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] gave them the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]] and said**, “I am **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/yahweh|Yahweh]], your God**, **who [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]] you from [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slavery]]** in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]]**. Do not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|gods]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Then God gave them the covenant and said**  - What God says next is the content of the covenant, that is, he tells the people the things that they must obey. This could be translated as, “Then God told them His covenant. He said” or, “Then God made this covenant with them:”
    * 


**Yahweh your God**  - In some languages it might be more natural to change the order and say “your God Yahweh.” Make sure it does not sound like the Israelites had more than one God. It should be clear that Yahweh is the only God. Another way to translate this would be, “Yahweh, who is your God” or, “your God, whose name is Yahweh.”
    * 


**who saved you from slavery**  - This could be translated as, “I freed you from slavery.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-05|>>]]**


===== The Commandments [13-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b6c633?nolink&640x360}}


“Do not make **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idols]]** and do not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** them, because **I, [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/yahweh|Yahweh]], am a jealous [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. **Do not use my name in a disrespectful way**. Be sure to keep the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sabbath|Sabbath day]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/holy|holy]]**. That is, do all your work in six days, for the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sabbath|seventh day]]** is a day for you to rest and **to remember me**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(God continues speaking to Moses.)


    * 


**I, Yahweh, am a jealous God**  - This could be translated as, “I, Yahweh, will be angry if you worship or honor anything besides me.” God strongly desires that his people love, serve, and obey Him more than anything or anyone else. He must be the only master of their lives.
    * 


**Do not use my name in a disrespectful way**  - This could be translated as, “Do not talk about me in a way that does not show respect and honor” or, “Talk about me in a way that gives me proper respect and honor.”
    * 


**seventh day**  - To translate this, it is best to use the number (“seventh”) rather than give the name of a specific day of the week.
    * 


**to remember me**  - This could be translated as, “to keep me in mind” or, “to honor me.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-06|>>]]**


===== More Commandments [13-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ead889?nolink&640x360}}


“**Honor**  your father and your mother. Do not murder. **Do not commit [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/adultery|adultery]]**. **Do not steal**. **Do not lie**. Do not desire to have your neighbor’s wife, his house, or anything that belongs to him.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


(God continues speaking to Moses.)


    * 


**Do not commit adultery**  - This could be translated as, “Do not have sexual relations with someone else's spouse” or, “Do not have marital relations with another man's wife or another woman's husband.” Be sure to translate this in a way that doesn't offend or embarrass people. Languages often have an indirect, polite way of saying this, such as, “Do not sleep with.”
    * 


**Do not lie**  - This means, “Do not say false things about other people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-07|>>]]**


===== The Stone Tablets [13-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=98cd41?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** wrote **these [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/ten-commandments|Ten Commandments]]** on two **stone tablets**  and gave them to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]**. **God also gave**  many other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|laws]]** and rules **to follow**. If the people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** these laws, God **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** that he would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|bless]]** and protect them. If they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** them, God would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punish]] them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**these Ten Commandments**  - This refers to the commands God gave to Moses for the Israelites to obey. They are listed in frames **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-05|[13-05]]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-06|[13-06]]]**.
    * 


**stone tablets**  - These were flat pieces of stone.
    * 


**God also gave**  - This can be translated as, “God also told them.”
    * 


**to follow**  - This can be translated as, “that they must obey” or, “that they must keep.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-08|>>]]**


===== The Tent of Meeting [13-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=009a3c?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** also gave the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]] a detailed description**of a tent he wanted them to make. **It was called**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tent-of-meeting|Tent of Meeting]]**, and it had two rooms, separated by a large curtain. Only the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** was allowed to go into **the room behind the curtain**, because **God lived there**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a detailed description**  - This could be translated as, “God described it in detail” or, “God told them exactly how He wanted them to make it.”
    * 


**It was called**  - This could be translated as, “They called it” or, “Moses called it.”
    * 


**the room behind the curtain**  - This room was hidden by the curtain. Some languages would call this room, “the room in front of the curtain.”
    * 


**God lived there**  - If this phrase would lead people to think that God was limited to living in the tent, here are some ways of translating it: “God was there” or, “God revealed Himself to humans there.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-09|>>]]**


===== The Altar [13-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=110db5?nolink&640x360}}


Anyone who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|God's law]]** could bring an animal **to the altar in front of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tent-of-meeting|Tent of Meeting]]** as a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. A **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priest]]** would kill the animal and burn it on the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/altar|altar]]**. **The [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/blood|blood]] of the animal that was sacrificed covered the person’s [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]** and made that person **clean in God's sight**. God chose **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses']]** brother, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]**, and Aaron's **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]** to be his priests.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God's law**  - This refers to all the commandments and instructions that God had told the Israelites to obey.
    * 


**to the Tent of Meeting**  - They did not bring the animal inside the Tent of Meeting, but to the altar in front of the Tent of Meeting. Be sure not to use an expression that means that they brought it inside.
    * 


**covered the person’s sin**  - When people brought animals to sacrifice, God chose to see the blood of the animals as a covering over their sin. This is like hiding something that is ugly or dirty by covering it.
    * 


**clean in God's sight**  - This could be translated as, “as if he did not have the sin according to God” or, “free of the punishment for breaking God's law.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-10|>>]]**


===== The People Sinned [13-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=18a74a?nolink&640x360}}


The people all agreed to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** the laws that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had **given them**, to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** only God, and to be **his special people**. But a short time after they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** to obey God, they **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]] terribly**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**given them**  - This could be translated as, “told them to obey.”
    * 


**his special people**  - From among all the nations, God had chosen the Israelites for his special purpose. This could be translated as “his special nation” or, “his own people” or, “the nation he chose to be his people.”
    * 


**a short time**  – The people sinned during the forty days that Moses was on the mountain with God.
    * 


**sinned terribly**  - They sinned in a way that was especially offensive to God. This could be translated as, “they sinned badly,” or “they did something that was very bad” or, “they did something bad that made God very angry.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-11|>>]]**


===== Make Us an Idol for Us [13-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=988393?nolink&640x360}}


For many days, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** was on top of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sinai|Mount Sinai]]** talking with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. **The people became tired of waiting**  for him to return. So they **brought gold**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]** and asked him to make an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idol]]** for them!


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**The people became tired of waiting**  - This could be translated as, “The people became impatient because he did not return quickly” or, “The people didn't want to wait any longer for him to return.”
    * 


**brought gold**  - These were objects and jewelry made of gold, which could be melted and formed into other things.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-12|>>]]**


===== The Golden Calf [13-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dfdfbb?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]] made a golden [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idol]]** in the shape of a calf. The people began to **wildly [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** the idol and make **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifices]]** to it! **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** was very angry with them because of their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]** and planned to destroy them. But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]** for them, and God **listened to his prayer**  and did not destroy them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**made a golden idol**  - Aaron took the things made of gold that the people had brought to him, melted them, combined them, and formed them into the shape of a calf.
    * 


**wildly worship**  - The people were sinning by worshiping the idol and also by doing sinful things as they worshiped it.
    * 


**listened to his prayer**  - God always hears prayer. In this situation, “listened” means that God agreed to do what Moses asked.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-13|>>]]**


===== Moses Was Angry [13-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bcd250?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** came down the mountain and saw the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idol]]**, he was so angry that he **smashed the stones**  on which **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had written the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/ten-commandments|Ten Commandments]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**smashed the stones**  - He threw the stones down on the ground and they broke up into little pieces.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-14|>>]]**


===== Moses Destroyed the Idol [13-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8d3291?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]] beat the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idol]] into powder**, threw the powder into some water and made the people drink the water. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** sent **a plague**  on the people and many of them died.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**beat the idol into powder**  - Moses utterly destroyed the idol by pounding it into fine particles.
    * 


**into some water**  - Moses scattered the gold powder over a large expanse of water.
    * 


**a plague**  - This could be translated as, “a terrible disease.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-15|>>]]**


===== Moses Prayed for Israel [13-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-13-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=c1dc90?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** climbed the mountain again and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/pray|prayed]]** that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgive]]** the people. God **listened to**  Moses and forgave them. **Moses wrote**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/ten-commandments|Ten Commandments]]** on new stone tablets to replace the ones he had broken. Then God led the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** away from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sinai|Mount Sinai]]** toward the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**.


//A Bible story from: Exodus 19-34//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**listened to**  - See how you translated this phrase in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-12|[13-12]]]**.
    * 


**Moses wrote**  - Moses chiseled the words into the stone using a tool.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/13-gods-covenant-with-israel|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-01|>>]]**


===== God Led Israel [14-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=eaf8c6?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** the laws he wanted them to obey as part of his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]]** with them, they left **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sinai|Mount Sinai]]**. God began leading them from toward the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**, which was also called **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**. The **pillar of cloud**  went ahead of them towards Canaan and they followed it.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**pillar of cloud**  - See how you translated this phrase in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__12-02|[12-02]]]**.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__13-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-02|>>]]**


===== The Canaanites' Idols [14-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=10ecb2?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]** that he would give the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]** to their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]**, but now there were many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/people-group|people groups]]** living there. They were called **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaanites]]**. The Canaanites did not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** or **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** God. They worshiped **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|false gods]]** and did many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|evil]]** things.


==== Translation Notes: ====


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 


**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-03|>>]]**


===== Destroy the Canaanites [14-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=4f2eed?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]**, “You must **get rid of**  all the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaanites]]** in the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**. **Do not make [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]] with them**and **do not marry them**. You must completely destroy all of their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idols]]**. If you do not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** me, **you will [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]] their idols**instead of me.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**get rid of**  - This could be translated as, “get them out of the land” or, “remove them from the land.”
    * 


**Do not make peace with them**  - This could be translated as, “Do not live peacefully among or alongside them” or, “Do not promise to live peacefully with them.”
    * 


**do not marry them**  - God did not want any Israelite person to marry any Canaanite person.
    * 


**you will worship their idols**  - If the Israelites became friends with the Canaanites and did not destroy the idols, they would be tempted to worship those idols instead of God. You could say, “you will end up worshiping” to make it clear that this would result from living so close to the Canaanites and learning their ways.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-04|>>]]**


===== The Twelve Spies [14-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=798cc1?nolink&640x360}}


When the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** reached the border of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** chose twelve men, one from each tribe of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. He gave the men instructions to go and **spy on the land**  to see what it was like. They were also to **spy on the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaanites]] to see if they were strong or weak**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**spy on the land**  - This could be translated as, “secretly get information about the land” or, “secretly learn about the land.” Part of the spies' task was to find out what kinds of food the land could produce.
    * 


**spy on the Canaanites**  - This could be translated as, “secretly get information about the people of Canaan” or, “secretly learn about the Canaanites.”
    * 


**to see if they were strong or weak**  - They wanted to know if the Canaanites were prepared to fight against them. This could be translated as, “to find out how powerful the Canaanite armies were.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-05|>>]]**


===== The Bad Report [14-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=09c8e0?nolink&640x360}}


The twelve men traveled through **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]** for forty days and then **they came back**. They told the people, “The land is very fertile and the crops are plentiful!” But ten of the spies said, “**The cities are very strong**  and **the people are giants**! If we attack them, they will certainly defeat us and kill us!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**they came back**  - They returned to where the rest of the Israelites were waiting, just outside the border of Canaan.
    * 


**The cities are very strong**  - The cities had strong walls around them, so it would be very difficult for the Israelites to attack them.
    * 


**the people are giants**  – This could be translated as, “the people are like giants compared to us!” or, “the people are much taller and stronger than we are!”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-06|>>]]**


===== Joshua and Caleb [14-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1f4f83?nolink&640x360}}


Immediately **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/caleb|Caleb]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]**, the other two spies, said, “It is true that the **people of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]** are tall and strong, but **we can certainly defeat them! [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] will fight for us**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**people of Canaan**  – This could be translated as, “the people who live in Canaan” or, “the Canaanites.”
    * 


**we can certainly defeat them! God will fight for us**  – To show the connection between these two statements, it may be necessary to say, “we can certainly defeat them because God will fight for us!”
    * 


**God will fight for us**  – This could be translated as, “God will fight alongside us and help us defeat them!” This makes it clear that the Israelites would also be fighting against the Canaanites.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-07|>>]]**


===== The People Rebelled [14-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7e1d01?nolink&640x360}}


But the people did not listen to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/caleb|Caleb]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]**. They became angry with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/aaron|Aaron]]** and said, “**Why did you bring us**  to **this horrible place**? We should have stayed in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/egypt|Egypt]] rather than be killed in battle and our wives and children made [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/servant|slaves]]**.” The people wanted to choose a different leader to take them back to Egypt.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Why did you bring us**  – This is not a real question. It is a way that some languages use to say, “You should not have brought us.”
    * 


**this horrible place**  - They considered Canaan to be “horrible” because they thought it was so dangerous that they would all be killed.
    * 


**rather than be killed in battle and our wives and children made slaves**  - This could be translated as, “If we fight against the Canaanites, they will kill us men and force our wives and children to be their slaves.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-08|>>]]**


===== God Spoke [14-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=99464b?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] was very angry**and **came to**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tent-of-meeting|Tent of Meeting]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** said, “Because you have rebelled against me, all of the people will have to **wander in the wilderness**. Except for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/caleb|Caleb]]**, everyone who is twenty years or older will die there and never enter the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**came to**  - God did not appear as a person, but came in some other form that showed his glory and power.
    * 


**wander in the wilderness**  - God would lead the people around in the wilderness with no specific destination until all of the adults who rebelled against him died.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-09|>>]]**


===== The People Ignored God [14-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=dfe989?nolink&640x360}}


When the people heard this, they were sorry **they had [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]]**. They took their weapons and went to attack the people of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]] warned them not to go**because **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] was not with them**, **but they did not listen to him**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**they had sinned**  - It may be necessary to add, “they had sinned by disobeying God's command to conquer the peoples of Canaan.”
    * 


**Moses warned them not to go**  - This means that Moses told them not to go to fight against the Canaanites because they would be in danger if they did that.
    * 


**God was not with them**  – In other words, God would not be with them to help them. Because of the Israelites' disobedience, God withdrew from them his presence, protection, and power.
    * 


**but they did not listen to him**  - They did not obey Moses. They went to attack the Canaanites anyway.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-10|>>]]**


===== The Canaanites Defeated Israel [14-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f0e620?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] did not go with them into this battle**, so they were defeated and many of them were killed. Then the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]] turned back from [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]** and **wandered through the wilderness**  for forty years.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God did not go with them into this battle**  - In other words, God did not help them in this fight.
    * 


**turned back from Canaan**  - They left Canaan and went back into the wilderness where they were before.
    * 


**wandered through the wilderness**  - They lived in the wilderness, and together they moved from place to place in that large, dry land, looking for food and water for themselves and their animals.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-11|>>]]**


===== Manna from Heaven [14-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6c9933?nolink&640x360}}


During the forty years that the people of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** wandered in the wilderness, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] provided for them**. He gave them **bread from heaven, called “manna.” He also sent flocks of quail**  (which are medium-sized birds) **into their camp**  so they could have meat to eat. During all that time, God kept their clothes and shoes from wearing out.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God provided for them**  – This could be translated as, “God gave them everything they needed for food, water, and shelter.”
    * 


**bread from heaven, called “manna”**  - This thin, bread-like food fell from the sky overnight onto the grass like dew. They called it “manna.” Almost every day the people gathered this “manna” and cooked it as their food.
    * 


**He also sent flocks of quail…camp**  - Another way to say this would be, “He also caused a large number of quails to fly into their camp.” If quails are unknown, a different, similar type bird could be used. Or it could be translated as, “a large number of medium-sized birds.”
    * 


**their camp**  - The place where the Israelites set up their tents to sleep in was called a “camp.” It was like a city with tents instead of buildings, and it could be moved around.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-12|>>]]**


===== Water from a Rock [14-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ef2d3d?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** even **miraculously gave them water from a rock**. **But despite all this**, the people of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** complained and grumbled against God and against **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]**. **Even so, God was still [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]] to his [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promises]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/abraham|Abraham]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/isaac|Isaac]]**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jacob|Jacob]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**miraculously gave them water from a rock**  - This could be translated, “by doing something that only God can do, he made water pour out of a rock so the people and animals could drink.”
    * 


**But despite all this**  - This could be translated as, “But even though God provided food, water, clothing, and everything that they needed.”
    * 


**Even so**  - This could be translated, “Even though the Israelites complained and grumbled against him.”
    * 


**God was still faithful to his promises**  - This could be translated, “God continued to do what he had told Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob he would do.” He provided their descendants with what they needed so they that could live and become a great nation and eventually own the land of Canaan.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-13|>>]]**


===== Moses Struck the Rock [14-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e7884c?nolink&640x360}}


Another time when the people did not have any water, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]**, “Speak to the rock, and water will come out of it.” But **Moses dishonored God**  in front of all the people **by hitting the rock twice with a stick instead of speaking to it**. Water came out of the rock for everyone to drink, but God was angry with Moses and said, “You will not enter the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Moses dishonored God**  - This could be translated, “Moses disobeyed God” or, “Moses disrespected God.” God had a specific way He wanted Moses to show the people God's power to provide for them. When Moses disobeyed God by doing it in a different way he showed a lack of respect for God.
    * 


**by hitting the rock twice with a stick instead of speaking to it**  - This can be translated as, “Moses did not speak to the rock; he hit it twice with a stick.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-14|>>]]**


===== At the Promised Land [14-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ebde9d?nolink&640x360}}


After the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** had wandered in the wilderness for forty years, all of them **who had [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebel|rebelled]] against [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** were dead.
