Then God led **the people**  to the edge of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]** again. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** was now very old, so God chose **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** to help him lead the people. God also **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** Moses that **one day**, he would send **another [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]] like Moses**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**who had rebelled against God**  - This could be translated, “who had refused to obey God when he told them to go into the Promised Land.”
    * 


**the people**  - That is, the children of the generation that died.
    * 


**one day**  - This means, “some time in the future.”
    * 


**another prophet like Moses**  - Like Moses, this man would be an Israelite, he would speak God's words to the people, and he would lead the people.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-15|>>]]**


===== The Death of Moses [14-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-14-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=8ab99d?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** to go to the top of a mountain so he could see the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**. Moses saw the Promised Land but God did not permit him to enter it. Then Moses died, and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]] mourned for thirty days**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** became their new leader. Joshua was a good leader because he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/trust|trusted]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** God.


//A Bible story from: Exodus 16-17; Numbers 10-14; 20; 27; Deuteronomy 34//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**mourned for thirty days**  - For thirty days all the people of Israel cried and showed that they were very sad that Moses had died.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/14-wandering-in-the-wilderness|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-01|>>]]**


===== The Two Spies [15-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d886f9?nolink&640x360}}


**At last it was time for**  the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** to **enter [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** sent **two spies to the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaanite]] city of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jericho|Jericho]]** that was **protected by strong walls**. In that city there lived a prostitute named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rahab|Rahab]]** who hid the spies and later helped them to **escape**. She did this because she **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/believe|believed]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. They **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** to protect Rahab and **her family**  when the Israelites would destroy Jericho.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**At last it was time for**  - “At last” means “finally” or, “after a long wait.” To make it clear what “time” refers to, you could say, “after they had wandered in the desert for 40 years, God finally permitted.”
    * 


**two spies to the Canaanite city of Jericho**  - This could be translated as, “two men to Jericho, a city in Canaan, to find out information about it.” Also see the notes for, “spy out the land” in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-04|[14-04]]]**.
    * 


**protected by strong walls**  - This could be translated as, “completely surrounded by thick, strong walls made of stone to protect it from their enemies.”
    * 


**escape**  – It is also possible to add, “escape from people in Jericho who wanted to harm them.”
    * 


**her family**  - Rahab asked for protection for her father, mother, brothers, and sisters. Use your word for family that includes these people.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__14-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-02|>>]]**


===== Crossing the Jordan River [15-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=fd8511?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** had to cross the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jordan-river|Jordan River]]** to enter into the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]**, “**Have the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priests]] go first**.” When the priests started to step into the Jordan River, **the water upstream stopped flowing**  so the Israelites could cross over to the other side of the river on dry ground.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Have the priests go first**  – For some languages it may be helpful to add, “Have the priests go before the rest of the people to cross the river.”
    * 


**the water upstream stopped flowing**  — In some languages it may be helpful to add, “and the water in front of them flowed away downstream.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-03|>>]]**


===== Marching around Jericho [15-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2b253b?nolink&640x360}}


**After the people crossed the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jordan-river|Jordan River]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]] how to attack**the powerful city of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jericho|Jericho]]**. The people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** God. Just as God told them to do, the soldiers and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priests]]** marched around the city of Jericho **once a day for six days**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**After the people crossed the Jordan River**  – In some languages it is better to say, “The people crossed the Jordan River and then…”
    * 


**how to attack**  – This could be translated as, “exactly what he should do to attack.”
    * 


**once a day for six days**  - That is, they went around the city one time every day for a total of six days.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-04|>>]]**


===== Shouting to God [15-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=57ebc1?nolink&640x360}}


Then on the seventh day, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites ]]** marched around the city seven more times. **While they marched around the city for the last time**, the soldiers shouted while the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest|priests]] blew their trumpets**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**While they marched around the city for the last time**  - This can be translated as, “During their final circuit around the city.”
    * 


**blew their trumpets**  - This could be translated as, “They sounded their trumpets” or, “They played their trumpets.” These trumpets were made out of ram's horns.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-05|>>]]**


===== The Walls Fell Down [15-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=61181c?nolink&640x360}}


Then the walls around **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jericho|Jericho]]** fell down! The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** destroyed everything in the city as **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had commanded. They only spared **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rahab|Rahab]]** and her family, who **became part of**  the Israelites. When the other people living in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]** heard that the Israelites had destroyed Jericho, they were terrified that the Israelites would attack them also.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**became part of**  - This can be translated as, “who then joined the Israelite community” or, “who then became members of the nation of Israel.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-06|>>]]**


===== The Gibeonites' Lie [15-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=452ffc?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had commanded the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** not to make a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]] treaty**with any of the people groups in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**. **But one of the Canaanite people groups, called the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gibeon|Gibeonites]]**, **lied to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]] and said**they were from a place far from Canaan. They asked Joshua to make a peace treaty with them. Joshua and the Israelites did not ask God **where the Gibeonites were from**. So Joshua made a peace treaty with them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**peace treaty**  – This is an agreement between two groups of people that they will not harm each other but will live in peace and help each other. This could be translated as, “peace agreement.”
    * 


**But one of the Canaanite people groups called the Gibeonites**  – Some languages may introduce this as, “But one day a Canaanite people group by the name of the Gibeonites …”
    * 


**lied to Joshua and said**  - This could be translated as, “They lied to Joshua by saying” or, “They falsely said to Joshua” or, “They falsely told Joshua.”
    * 


**where the Gibeonites were from**  - That is, “where the Gibeonites lived” or, “where the Gibeonites' home was.” “Gibeonites” means, “people of Gibeon.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-07|>>]]**


===== The Gibeonites in Danger [15-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b4a292?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** were angry when they found out that the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gibeon|Gibeonites]]** had deceived them, but they kept the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]]** treaty they had made with them because it was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promise]]** before **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**. Sometime later, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|kings]]** of another people group in **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaan]]**, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/amorite|Amorites]]**, heard that the Gibeonites had made a peace treaty with the Israelites, so they combined their armies into one large army and attacked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gibeon|Gibeon]]**. The Gibeonites **sent a message to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]] asking for help**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**sent a message to Joshua asking for help**  - This could be translated as, “sent some of their people to tell Joshua that they needed the Israelites to help defend them against their enemies.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-08|>>]]**


===== Israel Helped the Gibeonites [15-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=12a399?nolink&640x360}}


So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** gathered the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]]** army and they marched all night **to reach the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gibeon|Gibeonites]]**. In the early morning **they surprised the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/amorite|Amorite]] armies**and attacked them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**to reach the Gibeonites**  - That is, “to get to the Gibeonites” or, “to arrive at where the Gibeonites lived.” The Gibeonites lived in Canaan, but Canaan is big enough that it took all night for the Israelite army to travel from their camp to where the Gibeonites were.
    * 


**they surprised the Amorite armies**  - The Amorites did not know that the Israelites were coming to attack them.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-09|>>]]**


===== God Fought the Amorites [15-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=06a3ef?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] fought for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** that day. He **caused the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/amorite|Amorites]] to be confused**and he sent **large hailstones**  that killed many of the Amorites.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God fought for Israel**  - God fought on the side of Israel against Israel's enemies.
    * 


**caused the Amorites to be confused**  - This could be translated as, “made the Amorites panic” or, “caused the Amorites to be unable to fight together well.”
    * 


**large hailstones**  - This could be translated as, “very large balls of ice to come down from the sky.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-10|>>]]**


===== The Sun Stood Still [15-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=96cc8c?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** also caused the sun to stay in one place in the sky so that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** would have enough time to completely defeat the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/amorite|Amorites]]**. On that day, God won a great victory for Israel.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


//(There are no notes for this frame.)// 
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-11|>>]]**


===== Israel Defeated the Canaanites [15-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=13975c?nolink&640x360}}


After God defeated those armies, many of the other **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaanite]]** people groups gathered together to attack **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** and the Israelites **attacked and destroyed them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**attacked and destroyed them**  - This could be translated as, “fought against them and defeated them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-12|>>]]**


===== Dividing the Promised Land [15-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=749d3f?nolink&640x360}}


After this battle, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] gave each tribe of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]] its own section of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promised-land|Promised Land]]**. Then God **gave Israel [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]] along all its borders**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God gave…Land**  – this could be translated as, “God appointed each tribe its own plot of land” or, “God decided which part of the Promised Land each tribe of Israel would live on.”
    * 


**gave Israel peace along all its borders**  – This could be translated as, “God allowed the Israelites to experience peace with the other people groups that surrounded them” or. “the other countries around Israel.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-13|>>]]**


===== Joshua Renewed the Covenant [15-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-15-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=e9f1ad?nolink&640x360}}


**When [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]] was an old man**, he called all the people of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** together. Then Joshua reminded the people of their obligation to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/covenant|covenant]]** that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** had made with the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** at **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sinai|Sinai]]**. The people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** to **remain [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]] to God**and **follow [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|his laws]]**.


//A Bible story from: Joshua 1-24//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**When Joshua was an old man**  – It may be clearer to say, “Many years later, when Joshua was an old man.” Joshua was over 100 years old at this time.
    * 


**remain faithful to God**  - In other words, they would be loyal to God. They would worship and serve only God; they would not worship or serve any other gods.
    * 


**follow his laws**  - This means that the people would obey the laws that God had given them already as part of the covenant.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/15-the-promised-land|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-01|>>]]**


===== Israel Worshiped Idols [16-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f38402?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/joshua|Joshua]]** died, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] and did not drive out the rest of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/canaan|Canaanites]] or [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gods-law|God's laws]]**. The Israelites began to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** the Canaanite **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|gods]]** instead of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/yahweh|Yahweh]]**, **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/true|true]] God**. The Israelites had no **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]**, so everyone did **what they thought was right for them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**and did not drive out**  – This tells how they disobeyed God, so in some languages it may be better to start this as a new sentence, “They did not.”
    * 


**drive out the rest of the Canaanites**  - This can be translated, “fight with the rest of the Canaanites to force them to leave the land.”
    * 


**or obey God's laws**  - This means that the people also disobeyed the laws that God gave to the Israelites at Mount Sinai.
    * 


**the true God**  - That is, “the only real God.” Yahweh is the only one that people should worship.
    * 


**what they thought was right for them**  – This means that they all did whatever they wanted to do, including many evil things.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__15-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-02|>>]]**


===== Enemies Defeated Israel [16-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=403bee?nolink&640x360}}


Because the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** kept **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeying]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punished]]** them by allowing their enemies to defeat them. These enemies stole things from the Israelites, destroyed their property, and killed many of them. After many years of disobeying God and being oppressed by their enemies, the Israelites **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repented]]** and **asked God to rescue them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**asked God to rescue them**  - That is, they asked God to help them and to set them free from their enemies.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-03|>>]]**


===== The Deliverer [16-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=121f18?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] provided**a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/deliverer|deliverer]]** who rescued them from their enemies and **brought [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/peace|peace]]** to **the land**. But then **the people forgot about God**  and started **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiping]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idols]]** again. So God allowed the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]]**, a nearby enemy people group, to defeat them.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God provided**  - This could be translated as, “God chose” or, “God appointed” or, “God raised up.”
    * 


**brought peace**  - This could be translated as, “allowed the people to live without fear” or, “ended the fighting” or, “stopped their enemies from attacking them.”
    * 


**the land**  - That refers to Canaan, the Promised Land that God had given to Abraham.
    * 


**the people forgot about God**  - This means, “The people stopped thinking about God and ignored what he had commanded them.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-04|>>]]**


===== The Rule of Midian [16-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f2d693?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]]** took all of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites']] crops**for seven years. The Israelites were **so scared; they hid**  in caves so the Midianites would not find them. Finally, they **cried out**  to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]] them**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**crops**  - This refers to plants that the Israelites were growing in their gardens or fields for food.
    * 


**were so scared; they hid**  – This could be translated as, “were very afraid of the Midianites, so they hid.”
    * 


**cried out**  - This might be translated as, “they called out” or, “they prayed desperately.”
    * 


**save them**  – This might be translated as, “set them free” or, “rescue them from these enemies.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-05|>>]]**


===== An Angel Spoke to Gideon [16-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0d43ae?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, a man of Israel named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]** was **threshing grain secretly**  so the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]]** would not steal it. The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/angel|angel]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/yahweh|Yahweh]]** came to Gideon and said, “**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] is with you**, mighty warrior. Go and save **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** from the Midianites.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**threshing grain**  - The grain was wheat, which has a head of many small grains, or seeds, on the top of a thin stalk. “Threshing” is separating the seeds of the plant from the stalks by beating the heads of grain. The seeds are food, but the stalks are not.
    * 


**secretly**  - Gideon was threshing the grain in a hidden location, so the Midianites would not see him.
    * 


**God is with you**  – This means, “God is present with you in a special way” or, “God has plans to use you in a special way.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-06|>>]]**


===== Gideon Destroyed the Idol [16-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f18db8?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon's]]** father had an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/altar|altar]]** dedicated to an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idol]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told Gideon **to tear down**  that altar. But Gideon was **afraid of the people**, so he **waited until nighttime**. Then he tore down the altar and smashed it to pieces. He built a new altar to God near where the altar to the idol used to be and made a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifice]]** to God on it.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**to tear down**  - This means, “to violently bring down” or, “to take down and destroy.”
    * 


**afraid of the people**  - Gideon was afraid that his fellow Israelites who worshiped the same idol would be angry with him.
    * 


**waited until nighttime**  - Another way to say this would be, “waited until after dark.” Gideon smashed the altar at night when everyone was asleep so that no one would see him do it.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-07|>>]]**


===== Gideon Was Rescued [16-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=ce0392?nolink&640x360}}


The next morning the people saw that someone had torn down and destroyed the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/altar|altar]]**, and they were very angry. They went to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon's]]** house to kill him, but Gideon's father said, “**Why are you trying to help your [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|god]]**? **If he is a god, let him protect himself**!” Because he said this, the people did not kill Gideon.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Why are you trying to help your god?**  - This is not a real question that asks for information. Another way of saying this would be, “You should not be trying to help your god” or, “You should not need to help your god.”
    * 


**If he is a god, let him protect himself**  - This means, “If he were truly a god, he would be able to defend himself.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-08|>>]]**


===== Midian Attacked Israel Again [16-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=02d1bb?nolink&640x360}}


Then the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]] came again to steal from the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]**. There were so many of them that **they could not be counted**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]** called the Israelites together to fight them. Gideon asked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]****for two signs**  so he could be sure **that God would use him to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**came again to steal from the Israelites**  – This could be translated as, “came again to the Israelites' land to steal things from them.”
    * 


**they could not be counted**  - This could be translated as, “The number of the Midianites was too great to count” or, “it would be very difficult to count all of the Midianites.”
    * 


**for two signs**  - This could be translated as, “to do two miracles” or, “to make two impossible things happen.”
    * 


**that God would use him**  – This could be translated as, “that God would enable him” or, “that God would help him” or, “that God was calling him.”
    * 


**to save Israel**  - This could be translated as, “to rescue Israel from the Midianites.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-09|>>]]**


===== The Wet Cloth [16-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b14cc1?nolink&640x360}}


For the first **sign**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]** laid a cloth on the ground and asked **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** to **let the morning dew fall**  only on the cloth and not on the ground. **God did that**. The next night, he asked that the ground be wet but the cloth dry. God did that too. These two signs convinced Gideon that God would use him to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**sign**  - This could be translated as, “miracle” or, “impossible thing.”
    * 


**let the morning dew fall**  - This can be translated as, “make the morning dew appear” or, “make the morning dew come up.” “Dew” refers to the drops of water that appear on the ground in the morning. Dew naturally covers everything equally.
    * 


**God did that**  - This could be translated as, “God did what Gideon asked him to do.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-10|>>]]**


===== Too Many Soldiers [16-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=503054?nolink&640x360}}


**32,000 [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]] soldiers came to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]**, but **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told him this was **too many**. So Gideon sent home 22,000 who were afraid to fight. God told Gideon that he still had too many men. So Gideon sent all of them home **except for 300 soldiers**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**32,000 Israelite soldiers came to Gideon**  - Some languages might need to insert the following sentence at the beginning of the story: “Gideon called the Israelites to come fight against the Midianites.” See **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-08|[16-08]]]**.
    * 


**too many**  - This was more soldiers than God wanted for this fight. If that many solders fought and won, they would think that they won the battle with their own strength, and they would not know that God did it.
    * 


**except for 300 soldiers**  - This sentence could be translated as, “So Gideon allowed only 300 men to stay, and the rest of the men went home.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-11|>>]]**


===== The Midianite's Dream [16-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=726fd7?nolink&640x360}}


That night **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** told **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]**, “**Go down**  to the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianite]]** camp and when you hear what they say, you will **no longer be afraid**.” So that night, Gideon went down to the camp and heard a Midianite soldier telling his friend about **something he had [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/dream|dreamed]]**. The man’s friend said, “This dream means that Gideon's army will defeat the Midianite army!” When Gideon heard this, he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** God.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Go down**  - The Midianite soldiers were camping out in a valley and were at a lower elevation than the Israelite soldiers.
    * 


**you will no longer be afraid**  – That is, “you will stop being afraid.”
    * 


**something he had dreamed**  – That is, “something he had seen in a dream” or, “a dream he had had.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-12|>>]]**


===== Gideon's Army [16-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b95c90?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]** returned to his soldiers and gave each of them a **horn**, a clay pot, and **a torch**. They surrounded the camp where the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianite]]** soldiers were sleeping. Gideon's 300 men soldiers had the torches in the pots so the Midianites could not see the light of the torches.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**horn**  - This could be translated as, “trumpet” or, “ram's horn trumpet.” These horns came from a male sheep and were often used to call men for battle.
    * 


**a torch**  - This was probably a piece of wood wrapped with cloth and soaked in oil so that it could burn well. (This was not the modern torch that runs on batteries.)
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-13|>>]]**


===== The Attack [16-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=70b1ae?nolink&640x360}}


Then, all of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon's]]** soldiers broke their pots at the same moment, suddenly revealing the fire of the torches. They blew their horns and **shouted**, “**A sword for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] and for Gideon**!”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**shouted**  - This could be translated as, “yelled loudly” or, “said with a very loud voice.”
    * 


**sword**  - A sword is a weapon that has a long sharp blade and a handle at one end. People hold the handle and hit or stab the enemy with the sharp blade. If your people don't have a weapon just like this, you could translate it as a “long knife,” “machete” or, “bush knife.”
    * 


**A sword for God and for Gideon**  - This means, “We fight for God and for Gideon!”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-14|>>]]**


===== God Defeated the Midianites [16-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d30c38?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] confused the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]]**, so that they started attacking and killing each other. Immediately, **the rest of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]] were called**from their homes to come help chase the Midianites. They killed many of them and chased the rest of them out of the Israelites' land. 120,000 Midianites died that day. God had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|saved]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**God confused the Midianites**  - God caused the Midianites to be confused. They wanted to attack the Israelites, but instead, they attacked each other.
    * 


**the rest of the Israelites**  - This could be translated as, “many other Israelite men.” This refers to the soldiers previously sent home in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-10|[16-10]]]**.
    * 


**were called**  – That is, “were called out” or, “were summoned.” This sentence could also be translated as, “Gideon sent messengers to summon many other Israelite men from their homes.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-15|>>]]**


===== An Offering for Gideon [16-15] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-15.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=bee3f9?nolink&640x360}}


The people wanted to make **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]]** their **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]**. Gideon **did not allow them to do this**, **but he asked them**  for some of the gold rings that each of them had taken from the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/midian|Midianites]]**. The people gave Gideon a large amount of gold.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**did not allow them to do this**  - Gideon knew that it was better for the Israelites to have God as their king.
    * 


**but he asked them**  – This phrase starts with “but” because what he did next was not wise.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-16|>>]]**


===== Gideon Made an Idol [16-16] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-16.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=f247f3?nolink&640x360}}


Then **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/gideon|Gideon]] used the gold to make a special garment**like the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/priest-high|high priest]]** used to wear. But the people started **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiping]]** it as if it were an **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idol]]**. So **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punished]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** again because they worshiped idols. God allowed their enemies to defeat them. They finally asked God for help again, and God sent them another **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/deliverer|deliverer]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Gideon used the gold to make a special garment**  – This could be translated as, “Gideon melted down the gold objects the people had given him and formed a special garment out of that gold.”
    * 


**turned away from God**  - This could be translated as, “disobeyed God” or, “stopped worshiping God.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-15|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-17|>>]]**


===== Sin and Deliverance [16-17] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-17.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=399d3a?nolink&640x360}}


**This pattern repeated many times**: the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punish]]** them, they would **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repent]]**, and God would send a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/deliverer|deliverer]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/save|save]]** them. Over many years, God sent many deliverers who saved the Israelites from their enemies.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**This pattern repeated many times**  - This could be translated as, “These things kept happening again and again” or, “These things happened many times.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-16|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-18|>>]]**


===== Israel Wanted a King [16-18] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-16-18.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=2b8c22?nolink&640x360}}


**Finally**, the people **asked [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]] for a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]] like all the other nations had**. They wanted a king who was tall and strong, and who could lead them into battle. **God did not like this request**, but he gave them a king just as they had asked.


//A Bible story from: Judges 1-3; 6-8//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Finally**  - This could be translated as, “After their enemies attacked them many times” or, “After many years of being attacked by many different nations.”
    * 


**asked God for a king**  - This could be translated as, “demanded that God give them a king” or, “kept asking God for a king.”
    * 


**like all the other nations had**  - Other nations had a king. Israel wanted to be like them and have a king too.
    * 


**God did not like this request**  – This could be translated as, “God did not agree with what they had asked him for.” God knew that they were rejecting him as their ruler and were instead choosing to follow a human leader.
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-17|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/16-the-deliverers|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-01|>>]]**


===== Wicked King Saul [17-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=475367?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/saul|Saul]]** was the **first [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]] of [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. He was tall and handsome, just like the people wanted. Saul was a good king for the first few years that he ruled over Israel. But then he became a wicked man who did not **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obey]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, so God chose a different man who would **one day be king in his place**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**first king of Israel**  – This could be translated as, “first king to rule over Israel.”
    * 


**one day**  – This could be translated as, “some time in the future” or “years later.”
    * 


**be king in his place**  – Another way to say this would be, “take his place as king over Israel” or, “rule as king instead of him.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__16-18|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-02|>>]]**


===== David the Shepherd [17-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6455f8?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** chose a young **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelite]]** named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** to be **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** after **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/saul|Saul]]**. David was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/shepherd|shepherd]]** from the town of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bethlehem|Bethlehem]]**. At different times while he was **watching**  his father's **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sheep|sheep]]**, David had killed both a lion and a bear that had attacked the sheep. David was a **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/humble|humble]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/righteous|righteous]]** man who **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/trust|trusted]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]]** God.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**watching**  - That is, “caring for” or, “protecting” or, “taking care of.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-03|>>]]**


===== David Killed Goliath [17-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=747136?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** became a great soldier and leader. When David was still a young man, he fought against **a giant named Goliath**. Goliath was a trained soldier, very strong, and almost three meters tall! But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** helped David kill Goliath and save **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. After that, David won many victories over Israel's enemies, for which the people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praised]]** him.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**a giant named Goliath**  - The word “giant” here describes a person who is unusually large and powerful. Goliath was a huge soldier in an army that was fighting against Israel.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-04|>>]]**


===== Saul Chased David [17-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=929bc1?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/saul|Saul]]** became jealous of the people's **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|love]]** for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]**. Saul tried many times to kill him, so David hid from Saul. **One day**, Saul was looking for David so he could kill him. Saul went into the same cave where David was hiding from Saul, but Saul did not see him. David was now very close to Saul and could have killed him, but he did not. Instead, David cut off a piece of Saul's clothes **to prove to Saul**  that he would not kill him in order to become **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**to prove to Saul**  - That is, “to convince Saul” or, “to show Saul.”
    * 


**to become king**  – David would not dishonor God by killing the man that God placed as king over Israel.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-05|>>]]**


===== David Became King [17-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cf311c?nolink&640x360}}


Eventually, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/saul|Saul]]** died in battle, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** became **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. He was a good king, and the people **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/love|loved]]** him. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]]** David and **made him successful**. David fought many battles and God helped him defeat Israel's enemies. David conquered **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]** and made it **his capital city**. **During David’s reign**, Israel became powerful and wealthy.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**made him successful**  - That is, “helped him accomplish the good things he wanted to do.”
    * 


**his capital city**  - That is, “the capital city of his kingdom.” David lived in Jerusalem and ruled from there.
    * 


**During David’s reign**  - That is, “During the time when David was king over Israel” or, “During the time when David was ruling as king over Israel.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-06|>>]]**


===== David Wanted to Build a Temple [17-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=376aed?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** wanted to **build a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|temple]]** where all the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** could **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and offer him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifices]]**. For about 400 years, the people had been worshiping God and offering sacrifices to him at the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tent-of-meeting|Tent of Meeting]]** that **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/moses|Moses]]** had built.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**build a temple**  - David wanted to construct a permanent building for worshiping God that would replace the portable Tent of Meeting.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-07|>>]]**


===== God's Promise to David [17-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b4b911?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** sent **the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nathan|Nathan]]** to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** with this message, “Because you are a **man of war**, you will not build **this [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** for me. Your **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/son|son]]** will build it. But, I will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|bless]]** you greatly. Someone from your family will always rule as **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**, and the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]** will be one of your **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/descendant|descendants]]**!” The Messiah was God’s Chosen One who would save people of the world from **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**the prophet Nathan**  – It may be more natural in some languages to say, “a prophet named Nathan.”
    * 


**man of war**  - That is, “man who fights battles.” David killed many, many people in battle against the Israelites' enemies. God wasn't punishing David, but God wanted a man of peace to build the Temple where people would worship him.
    * 


**this Temple**  - That is, “this building for worship” or, “this place of worship.”
    * 


**from sin**  - That is, “from the terrible consequences of their sin.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-08|>>]]**


===== David Praised God [17-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=5f5ba2?nolink&640x360}}


When **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** heard **these words**, he immediately thanked and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/praise|praised]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** because he had **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]]** David **this great honor**  and many **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessings]]**. David did not know when God would do these things. But as it happened, the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israelites]]** would have to wait a long time before the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/messiah|Messiah]]** came, almost 1,000 years.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**these words**  - That is, “the words the prophet had just said.” This refers back to the promises in **[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-07|[17-07]]]**.
    * 


**this great honor**  - People who lived later would highly respect David because some of his descendants would be kings over Israel and one of them would be the Messiah.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-09|>>]]**


===== God Blessed David [17-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=6ecfc3?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]] ruled with [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/justice|justice]] and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithfulness]] for many years**, and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bless|blessed]]** him. However, **toward the end of his life**  he **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sinned]] terribly**against God.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**David ruled with justice and faithfulness for many years**  - This could be translated as, “When David ruled the people, for many years he did what was right and fair, and he was faithful to God.”
    * 


**toward the end of his life**  - This may be translated as, “when David was older” or “later on in David's life.”
    * 


**sinned terribly**  - That is, “sinned in a very evil way.” David's sin was especially evil.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-10|>>]]**


===== David and Bathsheba [17-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=db6958?nolink&640x360}}


**One day**, when all of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David's]]** soldiers were away from home fighting battles, he looked out from his palace and **saw**  a beautiful woman **bathing**. Her name was **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bathsheba|Bathsheba]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**One day**  - This phrase introduces an event that happened in the past, but does not state the specific time. Many languages have a similar way to begin telling a true story.
    * 


**saw**  - Bathsheba may have been bathing at her own house, but David's palace was very high and he was able to see over walls that were lower.
    * 


**bathing**  - This may be translated as, “taking a bath” or, “washing herself.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-09|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-11|>>]]**


===== David's Sin [17-11] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-11.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=797ab3?nolink&640x360}}


**Instead of looking away**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** sent someone to bring her to him. **He slept with her**  and sent her back home. A short time later **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bathsheba|Bathsheba]]** sent a message to David saying that she was pregnant.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**Instead of looking away**  - That is, David did not look away from the woman as she bathed, as he should have done.
    * 


**He slept with her**  - This is a polite way to say that David had sexual relations with Bathsheba.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-10|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-12|>>]]**


===== David Murdered Uriah [17-12] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-12.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=82e05a?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bathsheba|Bathsheba's]]** husband, a man named **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/uriah|Uriah]]**, was one of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David's]]** best soldiers. David called Uriah back from the battle and told him to **go be with his wife**. But Uriah refused to go home while the rest of the soldiers were in battle. So David sent Uriah back to the battle and told the general to place him **where the enemy was strongest**  so that he would be killed.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**go be with his wife**  - That is, “go home to be intimate with his wife.” David wanted people, especially Uriah, to believe that Bathsheba was pregnant with Uriah's child.
    * 


**where the enemy was strongest**  - That is, the location in the battle where the most fighting was going on.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-11|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-13|>>]]**


===== Nathan Rebuked David [17-13] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-13.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=0a7330?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/uriah|Uriah]]** was killed, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** married **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bathsheba|Bathsheba]]**. Later, she gave birth to David's son. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** was very angry about what David had done, so he sent the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/prophet|prophet]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/nathan|Nathan]]** to tell David how **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/evil|evil]]** his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]** was. David **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/repent|repented]]** of his sin and God **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/forgive|forgave]]** him. For the rest of his life, **David followed and [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/obey|obeyed]] God**, even in difficult times.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**what David had done**  - This refers to David's adultery with Bathsheba and his murder of her husband, Uriah.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-12|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-14|>>]]**


===== Solomon Was Born [17-14] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-17-14.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=d8dc7d?nolink&640x360}}


But as **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punishment]]** for **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David's]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**, his baby boy died. There was also **fighting in David’s family**  for the rest of his life, and **David’s power was greatly weakened**. Though David had been unfaithful to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]**, God was still **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]]** to his **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promises]]**. Later, David and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/bathsheba|Bathsheba]]** had another son, and they named him **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]**.


//A Bible story from: 1 Samuel 10; 15-19; 24; 31; 2 Samuel 5; 7; 11-12//


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**fighting in David’s family**  - This “fighting” was very serious. Among other things, one of his sons murdered another son and tried to take David's place as king while David was still reigning. If possible, use a word that conveys the intensity of this conflict within the family.
    * 


**David’s power was greatly weakened**  - This might be translated as, “David became less powerful” or, “David lost much of his authority.”
    * 


//A Bible story from//  - These references may be slightly different in some Bible translations.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-13|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/17-gods-covenant-with-david|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-01|>>]]**


===== God Made Solomon Wise [18-01] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-01.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=835f15?nolink&640x360}}


After many years, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** died, and his son **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]** began to rule over **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]**. **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** spoke to Solomon and asked him what he wanted most. When Solomon **asked for [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/wise|wisdom]]**, God was pleased and made him the wisest man in the world. Solomon learned many things and was a very wise **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/judge|judge]]**. God also made him very wealthy.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**asked for wisdom**  - This could be translated as, “asked God to make him wise.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__17-14|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-02|>>]]**


===== Solomon Built the Temple [18-02] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-02.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=a9c547?nolink&640x360}}


In **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jerusalem|Jerusalem]]**, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]** built the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]]** for which his father **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/david|David]]** had planned and gathered materials. People now **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worshiped]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and offered **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sacrifice|sacrifices]]** to him at the Temple instead of at the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/tent-of-meeting|Tent of Meeting]]**. God came and **was present in the Temple**, and he lived there **with his people**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**was present in the Temple**  – That is, “was present in the Temple in a special way.” Even though God was also present everywhere else at the same time, he made himself especially available to the people at the Temple.
    * 


**with his people**  - This could be translated as, “in the midst of his people” or, “among his people.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-01|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-03|>>]]**


===== Solomon Served Other Gods [18-03] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-03.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=7974a2?nolink&640x360}}


But **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]** loved women from other countries. He **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/disobey|disobeyed]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** by marrying many women, almost 1,000 of them! Many of these women came from foreign countries and **brought their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god-false|gods]] with them**and continued to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]]** them. When Solomon was old, he also worshiped their gods.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**brought their gods with them**  - They brought their idols and their methods of worshiping idols with them to Israel.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-02|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-04|>>]]**


===== The Kingdom Would Divide [18-04] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-04.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=afd0db?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** was angry with **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]** and, **as a [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punishment]] for Solomon’s unfaithfulness, he [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/promise|promised]] to divide**the nation of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|Israel]]** into two **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdoms]]** after Solomon’s death.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**as a punishment for Solomon's unfaithfulness, he promised to divide**  – This could be translated as, “to punish Solomon for being unfaithful to him, God solemnly said that he would divide.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-03|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-05|>>]]**


===== Rehoboam Became King [18-05] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-05.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=cc7ad6?nolink&640x360}}


After **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]** died, his son, **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rehoboam|Rehoboam]]**, became **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]**. Rehoboam was a foolish man. All the people of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|nation of Israel]]** came together to **confirm him as king**. They complained to Rehoboam that Solomon had made them do a lot of hard work and pay a lot of taxes.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**confirm him as king**  - That is, “tell him that they were glad he was king and that they would do what he said.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-04|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-06|>>]]**


===== Rehoboam's Foolish Answer [18-06] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-06.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=1418ec?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rehoboam|Rehoboam]]****foolishly answered**  them, “You thought my father **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/solomon|Solomon]]** made you work hard, but I will make you work harder than he did, and I will **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/punish|punish]]** you more harshly than he did.”


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**foolishly answered**  - Rehoboam's answer was harsh, and caused the people to turn against him.
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-05|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-07|>>]]**


===== Israel Rebelled against Judah [18-07] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-07.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=915c4b?nolink&640x360}}


Ten of the **tribes of the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|nation of Israel]] [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebel|rebelled]] against [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rehoboam|Rehoboam]]**. Only two tribes **remained [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/faithful|faithful]] to him**. These two tribes became the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-judah|kingdom of Judah]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**tribes of the nation of Israel**  - The descendants of each of Jacob's twelve sons had become a “tribe” or very large family group in the nation of Israel. Everyone in Israel belonged to one of the twelve tribes.
    * 


**rebelled against Rehoboam**  – That is, “refused to follow Rehoboam as their king.” It might help to start this sentence with, “So” or, “Because of that” or, “Because of what Rehoboam said.”
    * 


**remained faithful to him**  – That is, “stayed loyal to him” or, “continued to support him as king.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-06|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-08|>>]]**


===== Jeroboam Ruled Israel [18-08] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-08.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=b6fe7f?nolink&640x360}}


The other ten tribes of the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/israel|nation of Israel]]** that rebelled against **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rehoboam|Rehoboam]] appointed a man named [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jeroboam|Jeroboam]] to be their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/king|king]]**. They **set up their [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdom]]** in the northern part of the land and were called the **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-israel|kingdom of Israel]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**set up their kingdom**  - This may be translated as, they “established” or, “built” their kingdom. This sentence may also be translated as, “They separated themselves from the other two tribes and lived in the northern part of the land, and they called their country 'Israel.'”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-07|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-09|>>]]**


===== Jeroboam Made an Idol [18-09] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-09.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=79d8c2?nolink&640x360}}


**[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/jeroboam|Jeroboam]]** **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/rebel|rebelled]]** against **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/god|God]]** and **caused the people to [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/sin|sin]]**. He built two **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/idol|idols]]** for his people to **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/worship|worship]] instead of worshiping God at the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/temple|Temple]] in the [[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-judah|kingdom of Judah]]**.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    * 


**caused the people to sin**  - This could be translated as, “led the people to sin” or, “motivated the people to sin.” Rehoboam led the people into sin by making idols for them to worship.
    * 


**instead of worshiping God at…Judah**  - This can be translated as, “so that they would not worship God at” or, “instead of going to the kingdom of Judah to worship God at the Temple.”
**[[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-08|<<]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/18-the-divided-kingdom|Up]] | [[http://door43.org/en/obs-training/sandbox/larrysallee/obs-training-text-and-notes#plugin_include__en__obs-training__frames__18-10|>>]]**


===== Israel and Judah at War [18-10] =====


{{http://door43.org/_media/en/obs/obs-18-10.jpg?w=640&h=360&tok=59a731?nolink&640x360}}


The **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom|kingdoms]]** of **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-judah|Judah]]** and **[[http://door43.org/en/key-terms/kingdom-of-israel|Israel]]** became enemies and often fought against each other.


==== Translation Notes: ====


    *
